## 康普顿散射下湮没光对中的量子相关性量子化

**Original Title:** Quantifying Quantum Correlations in Annihilation Photon Pairs under Compton Scattering

**Authors:** Z. AskariPour Ravari, Z. Riazi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29035v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29035v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-27


### 摘要

我们对连续康普顿散射事件期间由仲正电子衰变产生的511 keV量子对中极化纠缠和量子相干性的演变进行了理论研究。我们从最大纠缠贝尔态开始，采用广义斯托克斯-穆勒形式主义来推导单、双和三康普顿散射后的双量子密度矩阵，明确考虑极向和方位角散射几何形状。使用这个框架，我们通过并发性（作为纠缠的衡量标准）和$l_1$-规范（作为一致性的衡量标准）量化量子相关性的退化。我们的结果表明，纠缠对散射几何形状高度敏感，并在直角散射附近消失，而即使在纠缠完全消失的区域中，量子相干性仍然是有限的。这些发现提供了对湮没光对中依赖于极化的退相干的统一描述，并澄清了纠缠和相干在现实双量子相互作用中的独特作用。这些结果与量子增强正电子发射断层扫描相关，并强调了量子资源在散射主导媒体中的持久性。


### Abstract

We present a theoretical study of the evolution of polarization entanglement and quantum coherence in 511 keV photon pairs produced by para-positronium decay during successive Compton scattering events. We start with a maximally entangled Bell state and employ the generalized Stokes-Mueller formalism to derive the two-photon density matrix following single-, double-, and triple-Compton scattering, explicitly considering both polar and azimuthal scattering geometries. Using this framework, we quantify the degradation of quantum correlations through concurrence (as a measure of entanglement) and the $l_1$-norm (as a measure of coherence). Our results demonstrate that entanglement is highly sensitive to the scattering geometry and disappears near right-angle scattering, while quantum coherence remains finite even in regimes where entanglement vanishes completely. These findings provide a unified description of polarization-dependent decoherence in annihilation photon pairs and clarify the distinct roles of entanglement and coherence in realistic two-photon interactions. These results are relevant for quantum-enhanced positron emission tomography and highlight the persistence of quantum resources in scattering-dominated media.


---


## 连续监测中的精确Hilbert空间历经性

**Original Title:** Exact Hilbert-space ergodicity from continuous monitoring

**Authors:** Yue Wu, Yuzhi Tong, Liang Mao, Pengfei Zhang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29042v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29042v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-27


### 摘要

人们普遍认为量子进化会推动量子多体系统走向平衡。这一期望通常被一般量子动力学的Hilbert空间遍寻性所证明，即纯状态进化在物理约束下均匀探索Hilbert空间的想法。通过要求相关的状态系综形成哈尔随机系综，或其更结构化的概括，斯克罗吉系综，可以使这样的陈述变得严格。在这封信中，我们报告了在连续监控的量子多体系统中出现的精确的Hilbert空间遍寻性。对于任何目标密度矩阵$Sigma $，我们构建了一个连续监控的系统，为此我们严格证明了$Sigma $的斯克罗吉系综是量子轨迹的唯一后期平衡分布。值得注意的是，这只要求监控中的跳跃操作符形成变形的单一1设计，这是一个似乎比完全历经弱得多的条件。我们通过模拟平衡状态为热状态的连续监测系统来数字证明我们的预测。我们的结果为Hilbert空间的出现建立了严格的机制，并为其量子器件的研究提供了一条实用的路线。


### Abstract

Quantum evolution is generally expected to drive a quantum many-body system toward equilibrium. This expectation is often justified by the Hilbert-space ergodicity of generic quantum dynamics, namely, the idea that pure-state evolution explores Hilbert space uniformly up to physical constraints. Such a statement can be made rigorous by requiring the associated state ensemble to form the Haar-random ensemble, or its more structured generalization, the Scrooge ensemble. In this Letter, we report the emergence of exact Hilbert-space ergodicity in a continuously monitored quantum many-body system. For any target density matrix $σ$, we construct a continuously monitored system for which we rigorously prove that the Scrooge ensemble of $σ$ is the unique late-time equilibrium distribution of quantum trajectories. Remarkably, this requires only that the jump operators in the monitoring form a deformed unitary 1-design, a seemingly much weaker condition than full ergodicity. We numerically demonstrate our predictions by simulating continuously monitored systems whose equilibrium states are thermal states. Our results establish a rigorous mechanism for the emergence of Hilbert-space ergodicity and provide a practical route for its investigation on quantum devices.


---


## 局部协变子索似乎是量子电路的基础

**Original Title:** Localized Covariant Quantities Appear To Underlie Quantum Circuits

**Authors:** Ken Wharton, Roderick Sutherland, Titus Amza, James Saslow

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29079v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29079v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-27


### 摘要

尽管纠缠态载体无法用局部化在空间和时间上的变量来完全描述，但任何给定的纠缠实验都可以从具有明确位置的基本量子电路组件构建。我们分析了此类量子电路，并提供了证据表明局部弱值包括与每个单独量子位相关的协变张量。即使状态严重纠缠，当其他量子位被测量或穿过远处的电路元件时，这些张量也不会进化或崩溃。因此，可以从不同的参考系来看待它们，而不会相互矛盾。此外，它们在任何回路中的进化总是遵循协变动力学规则。弱值受到过去和未来的约束，因此协变量只能通过“同时”考虑整个电路来确定，就像在行动原则中一样，结合未来的测量基础以避免标准的不去定理。由于这些结果适用于一组通用量子门，因此这项工作支持了这样的说法：任何量子电路都可以被赋予一个与我们对经典时空的理解兼容的现实的、较低级别的描述。


### Abstract

Although entangled state vectors cannot be fully described in terms of variables localized in space and time, any given entanglement experiment can be built from basic quantum circuit components with well-defined locations. We analyze such quantum circuits and present evidence that the local weak values comprise a covariant tensor associated with each individual qubit. Even if the state is massively entangled, these tensors do not evolve or collapse when other qubits are measured or pass through distant circuit elements. They can therefore be viewed from different reference frames without contradiction. Furthermore, their evolution through any circuit always obeys covariant dynamical rules. Weak values are subject to both past and future constraints, so the covariant quantities can only be determined by considering the entire circuit "all-at-once", as in action principles, incorporating the future measurement basis to avoid the standard no-go theorems. Because these results hold for a set of universal quantum gates, this work lends support to the claim that any quantum circuit can be assigned a realistic, lower-level description compatible with our understanding of classical spacetime.


---


## 经典张量网络模拟的阴影断层扫描

**Original Title:** Shadow tomography for classical tensor network simulations

**Authors:** Jiace Sun, Garnet Kin-Lic Chan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29133v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29133v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

阴影层析成像已经成为一个强大的工具，估计可观的量子计算机从少量的样本。我们表明，阴影断层扫描启发的想法可以提供类似的改进的样本缩放，以估计在经典计算机上的张量网络状态的观测值后，适当的适应。我们为自旋（玻色子）和费米子系统开发策略，根据张量网络的收缩要求量身定制，并根据特定的任务和系统类型，生成$O（N）$到$O（N^{3}）$（其中$N$是系统大小）的缩放改进因子。对于重要和困难的任务，评估的期望值的远程相互作用哈密顿量，我们实现了最佳的$O（1）$的整体缩放（对数因子）为任意固定的相对蒙特卡罗误差在自旋和费米子系统。此外，我们还表明，影子估计器在变分优化任务中提供了比标准蒙特卡罗估计器更稳定的观测量梯度。我们通过模拟具有远程相互作用的系统（包括2D远程海森堡模型和从头算量子化学Hamilton）来证明实际优势。


### Abstract

Shadow tomography has appeared as a powerful tool for estimating observables on quantum computers from a small number of samples. We show that shadow-tomography-inspired ideas can offer similarly improved sample scaling for estimating observables on tensor network states on classical computers after proper adaptation. We develop strategies for both spin (bosonic) and fermionic systems, tailored to the contraction requirements of tensor networks, and generate scaling improvements of factors of $O(N)$ to $O(N^{3})$ (where $N$ is system size), depending on the specific task and system type. For the important and difficult task of evaluating the expectation value of long-range interacting Hamiltonians, we achieve the optimal $O(1)$ overall scaling (up to logarithmic factors) for an arbitrarily fixed relative Monte Carlo error in both spin and fermionic systems. Additionally, we show that shadow estimators offer more stable gradients of observables in variational optimization tasks than standard Monte Carlo estimators. We demonstrate practical advantage by simulating systems with long-range interactions, including the 2D long-range Heisenberg model and an ab-initio quantum chemistry Hamiltonian.


---


## 可观测量代数的量子扰乱：$\mathbb{Z}_2$-对称情况

**Original Title:** Quantum scrambling of algebras of observables: the $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetric case

**Authors:** Paolo Zanardi, J. Karson Lewis

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29137v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29137v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

我们考虑整个一类可观察代数$\mathcalA $的正量子扰频，其交换子${\mathcalA}'=\mathbb{C}\mathbb{Z}_2$是由埃尔米特对合$S$生成的，即，平价运算符。我们采用两种不同但相关的加扰措施：（a）在[Andreadakis、Anand和Zanardi，Phys. Rev. A 107，042217（2023）]中引入的代数超时序相关器（A-OTEC），和（b）斯莱特决定型量，称为Plücker保真度，通过将运算符代数嵌入到更高维度的投射运算符空间中获得。这两种测量都承认了代数与其动态图像之间的距离的简单几何解释。此外，它们可以用酉的$\mathbb{Z}_2$-破缺分量的范数来表示，而这又由$\mathbb{Z}_2$生成元$S$的时间自相关函数控制。在一般情况下，我们推导出A-OTOC和Plücker保真度的精确表达式，以及它们对随机酉的值。对于哈密顿生成的通道，我们计算它们的长时间平均值，以及这些长时间平均值的随机生成器$S$的典型值。最后，我们数值探讨我们的形式主义的结果，在不同的阶段和不同的物理宇称算子的相互作用的自旋链。


### Abstract

We consider unitary quantum scrambling for an entire class of observable algebras $\mathcal A$ whose commutant ${\mathcal A}'=\mathbb{C}\mathbb{Z}_2$ is generated by a Hermitian involution $S$, i.e., a parity operator. We adopt two different, although related, scrambling measures: (a) the algebraic out-of-time-order correlator (A-OTOC) introduced in [Andreadakis, Anand, and Zanardi, Phys. Rev. A 107, 042217 (2023)], and (b) a Slater-determinant-type quantity, dubbed the Plücker fidelity, obtained by embedding operator algebras into a higher-dimensional projective operator space. Both measures admit a simple geometric interpretation in terms of distances between algebras and their dynamical images. Moreover, they can be expressed in terms of the norm of the $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetry-breaking component of the unitary, which is in turn controlled by the time autocorrelation function of the $\mathbb{Z}_2$ generator $S$. We derive exact expressions for the A-OTOC and the Plücker fidelity in the general case, as well as their values for a random unitary. For Hamiltonian-generated channels, we compute their long-time averages, as well as the typical values of these long-time averages for random generators $S$. Finally, we numerically explore the results of our formalism for interacting spin chains in different phases and for different physical parity operators.


---


## 膨胀宇宙中耦合三模压缩真空的高斯量子操纵

**Original Title:** Gaussian quantum steering of coupled three-mode squeezed vacuum in an expanding universe

**Authors:** Guang-Wei Mi, Xiaofen Huang, Tinggui Zhang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29144v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29144v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

耦合三模压缩真空是一种代表性的多模压缩高斯态，具有独特的可操纵性。这项工作研究了膨胀宇宙下耦合三模压缩真空的高斯量子操纵分布。由于内外时空区域之间的因果分离，爱丽丝、鲍勃和查理无法访问事件视界后面的量子信息。我们分别分析物理可及和不可及模式的转向行为。我们的分析表明，更大的总平均量子数和动量，加上减小的膨胀体积和膨胀率，可以增强量子操纵强度。值得注意的是，当超过关键阈值参数$ph $时，物理不可访问模式的高斯量子操纵会经历“猝死”现象。这些结果为弯曲时空中的量子相关性提供了新的见解。


### Abstract

The coupled three-mode squeezed vacuum is a representative multimode squeezed Gaussian state featuring unique steerability. This work investigates Gaussian quantum steering distributions of the coupled three-mode squeezed vacuum under an expanding universe. Due to causal separation between the interior and exterior spacetime regions, quantum information behind the event horizon is inaccessible to Alice, Bob and Charlie. We separately analyze steering behaviors for physically accessible and inaccessible modes. Our analysis shows that greater total mean photon number and momentum, combined with reduced expansion volume and expansion rate, enhance quantum steering strength. Notably, Gaussian quantum steering for physically inaccessible modes undergoes the "sudden death" phenomenon when a critical threshold parameter $φ$ is exceeded. These results deliver novel insights into quantum correlations in curved spacetime.

## 统计壳模型的嵌入随机矩阵集合：$q$-范式的操作

**Original Title:** Embedded Random Matrix Ensembles to Statistical Shell Model: Operation of $q$-normal forms

**Authors:** V. K. B. Kota, N. D. Chavda, Manan Vyas

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29210v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29210v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

嵌入式随机矩阵合奏在核壳模型空间中运行，核子占据有限的单粒子轨道集并通过两体相互作用相互作用，构成了统计壳模型的基础。在足够强的相互作用下，壳模型空间中的水平密度接近高斯形式，而转移强度分布接近二元高斯形式。在实践中，通过球形配置（$\tilde{m}$）和角动量$J$（在适当的情况下也包括isopin）进行划分至关重要。由此产生的统计光谱或统计壳模型过去曾成功地应用于核级密度、轨道占据、$β$-衰变矩阵元素等的一些研究中。除了这些之外，最近人们认识到嵌入式集合，在更好的近似下，实际上生成$q$-正态（$q=1$给出高斯，$q=0$维格纳半圆）表示特征值密度，二元$q$-转移强度的规范型和条件$q$-强度函数的规范型。然后，这些允许我们使用$q$-正常形式开发统计壳模型。本文简要回顾了嵌入式合奏和统计壳模型的这些新进展。还使用一些例子描述了$q$参数在生成一般量子多粒子系统统计性质中的作用。


### Abstract

Embedded random matrix ensembles operating in nuclear shell model spaces, with nucleons occupying a finite set of single particle orbits and interacting via a two-body interaction, form the basis for statistical shell model. With sufficiently strong interaction, the level densities in shell model spaces take close to a Gaussian form and transition strength distributions close to a bivariate Gaussian form. In practice, partitioning via spherical configurations ($\tilde{m}$) and angular momentum $J$ (also isospin where appropriate) are essential. The resulting statistical spectroscopy or statistical shell model was applied successfully in the past in some studies of nuclear level densities, orbit occupancies, $β$-decay matrix elements and so on. Going beyond these, recently it is recognized that embedded ensembles, in a better approximation, generate in-fact $q$-normal form ($q=1$ gives Gaussian and $q=0$ Wigner's semi-circle) for density of eigenvalues, bivariate $q$-normal form for transition strengths and conditional $q$-normal form for strength functions. These then allow us to develop statistical shell model with $q$-normal forms. These new developments in embedded ensembles and statistical shell model are briefly reviewed in this paper. Also described, using some examples, is the role of the $q$ parameter in generating statistical properties of general quantum many-particle systems.


---


## 开放量子系统中直接稳态估计的Rodeo过滤

**Original Title:** Rodeo Filtering for Direct Steady-State Estimation in Open Quantum Systems

**Authors:** Hyeonjun Yeo, Jongin Jeong, Soyoung Shin, Ha Eum Kim

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29218v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29218v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

计算开放量子系统的非平衡稳态在传统计算机上是一项具有挑战性的任务，激励量子算法进行直接稳态估计。一个自然的路线是将稳态视为刘维利安的零模式，并在光谱上孤立这个部门。我们将此任务表述为已知零部门投影问题，并使用Rodeo算法实现相应的过滤器，该算法通过重复受控进化和测量条件过滤步骤执行随机频谱过滤。在稳态设置中，过滤器可以直接以已知的零本征值为中心，从而避免通用本征状态准备中所需的谱搜索。与相同投影的基于阶段估计的实现相比，Rodeo方法能够在失败时重新启动，并将过滤成本和受控进化深度的目标误差依赖性从乘势定律减少到了对log。随着埃尔米特刘维利安嵌入的频谱分离度的增加，这一优势变得更加明显，从而允许Rodeo过滤在适度的受控进化深度上已经优于阶段估计过滤。我们的结果将Rodeo过滤确定为开放量子系统中估计稳态可观测量的资源高效基元。


### Abstract

Computing non-equilibrium steady states of open quantum systems is a challenging task on conventional computers, motivating quantum algorithms for direct steady-state estimation. A natural route is to regard the steady state as the zero mode of the Liouvillian and to isolate this sector spectrally. We formulate this task as a known-zero-sector projection problem and implement the corresponding filter using the Rodeo algorithm, which performs stochastic spectral filtering through repeated controlled evolutions and measurement-conditioned filtering steps. In the steady-state setting, the filter can be centered directly at the known zero eigenvalue, avoiding the spectral search required in generic eigenstate preparation. Compared with a phase-estimation-based implementation of the same projection, the Rodeo approach enables restart on failure and reduces the target-error dependence of the filtering cost and controlled-evolution depth from power-law to logarithmic. This advantage becomes more pronounced as the spectral separation of the Hermitian Liouvillian embedding increases, allowing Rodeo filtering to outperform phase-estimation filtering already at modest controlled-evolution depths. Our results identify Rodeo filtering as a resource-efficient primitive for estimating steady-state observables in open quantum systems.

## 虚构伪信息编码时间方向

**Original Title:** Imaginary pseudo entropy encodes temporal orientation

**Authors:** Tatsuhiro Misumi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29235v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29235v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

不同时间量子状态之间的伪熵通常很复杂，但其虚部缺乏有界的操作意义。我们表明，经过校准的复制干涉仪将伪雷尼相转换为直接可测量的过渡方向记录。与副本可见性一起，它准确确定了前向和后向辅助输出之间的轨迹距离，从而确定了Helstrom最优的单次射击成功概率。在短时间内，模和物理Hamilton的对称化协方差设定了初始的可互换性响应。在任何常见的量子通道下，相应的取向信息只会减少，以Petz恢复为特征的平等。因此，虚伪信息记录了时间方向之间的可逆差异，而粗粒化可以使该记录的损失不可逆转。


### Abstract

Pseudo entropy between quantum states at different times is generally complex, yet its imaginary part has lacked a bounded operational meaning. We show that a calibrated replica interferometer converts the pseudo-Rényi phase into a directly measurable record of transition orientation. Together with replica visibility, it exactly determines the trace distance between forward and backward ancilla outputs and hence the Helstrom-optimal single-shot success probability. At short times, the symmetrized covariance of the modular and physical Hamiltonians sets the initial distinguishability response. Under any common quantum channel, the corresponding orientation information can only decrease, with equality characterized by Petz recovery. Imaginary pseudo entropy therefore records a reversible distinction between temporal orientations, while coarse graining can make the loss of that record irreversible.


---


## 多环芳香族化合物的QmFT：平衡嵌入底态保真度和实验间隙估计

**Original Title:** QmDFT for Polycyclic Aromatics: Balancing Embedding Ground-State Fidelity and Experimental Gap Estimation

**Authors:** N. Manglani, Tejjan Arora, Samrit Maity, Ranjit Thapa, Shashank Sharma, Sanjay Wandhekar

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29245v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29245v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

量子嵌入密度泛函理论（QmDFT）嵌入提供了一种高度可扩展的方法，以改善大型高度相关的π共轭系统的治疗。然而，估计先进的多环芳烃（PAHs）的电子结构特性需要先进的交换相关泛函，频繁地触发收敛不稳定性，在嵌入周期。   在这项工作中，我们引入了自适应阻尼和直接反演的迭代子空间（DIIS）加速协议，稳定的嵌入过程，使强大的集成的混合泛函，如B3 LYP和CAM B3 LYP。使用10个选定的多环芳烃（线性和融合）分子作为基准。我们展示了一个明确的功能依赖性的底态能量学和前沿轨道间隙估计。虽然基于LDA的方法在FT参考能方面与FCI产生了近乎定量的一致性，并且得到了热化学异化基准的进一步支持，而B3 LY P与实验E0-0转变值的一致性显着提高。这种映射使我们能够绕过E0 0值的显式激励状态计算，从而显着减少计算负担。   在筛选的混合功能中，CAM B3 LY P提供了平衡的整体性能。我们的结果建立了稳定的QmFT框架，并为多环芳烃和相关低维pi-偶联材料的量子嵌入研究的功能选择提供了有用的指导。


### Abstract

Quantum Embedding density functional theory (QmDFT) embedding offers a highly scalable approach to improve treatment for large highly correlated pi conjugated systems. However, estimating advanced electronic structure properties in polycyclic aromatic hydrocarbons (PAHs) needs advanced exchange correlation functionals that frequently trigger convergence instabilities during the embedding cycle.
  In this work, we introduce an adaptive damping and direct inversion in the iterative subspace (DIIS) accelerated protocol that stabilizes the embedding procedure, enabling robust integration of hybrid functionals like B3LYP and CAM B3LYP. Using 10 selected PAHs (linear and fused) molecules as a benchmark. We demonstrate a clear functional-dependent ground-state energetics and frontier-orbital gap estimation. While LDA based approaches yield near-quantitative agreement with FCI in DFT reference energies and is further supported by thermochemical isomerization benchmarks, while B3LYP provide significantly improved agreement with experimental E0-0 transition values. This mapping allows us to bypass explicit excited-state calculations for E0 0 values, thereby significantly reducing computational overhead.
  Among the hybrid functionals screened, CAM B3LYP offers a balanced overall performance. Our results establish a stable QmDFT framework and provide useful guidance for functional selection for quantum embedding studies of PAHs and related low-dimensional pi-conjugated materials.
