## 利用Lax对散射求解非线性薛定格方程的量子算法

**Original Title:** Quantum algorithm for the nonlinear Schrödinger equation via the Lax-pair scattering

**Authors:** Chenjia Zhu, Zhaoyuan Meng, Yousheng Zhang, Yue Yang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29276v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29276v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

非线性薛定谔方程（NLSE）控制着广泛的波动现象，包括深水波、量子湍流和孤子。这些系统固有的多尺度时空耦合对经典的高保真数值模拟造成了严重的计算瓶颈。虽然量子计算提供了指数加速的潜力，但其酉动力学对解决NLSE提出了根本挑战。我们提出了一个基于Lax对散射的量子框架来求解一维NLSE。具体来说，物理场首先通过量子直接散射电路映射到光谱空间。经过脱钩的线性时间演变，通过利用量子奇异值变换的逆散射变换来重建物理解。由于时间演变是在散射域中以分析方式执行的，因此该框架绕过了迭代时间步进，使其对于长期模拟非常有利。为了证明这种方法的准确性和噪音复原力，我们在量子模拟器上模拟了量子噪音、两个孤立子碰撞、呼吸动力学和调制不稳定性下的高斯波包。


### Abstract

The nonlinear Schrödinger equation (NLSE) governs a broad class of wave phenomena, including deep-water waves, quantum turbulence, and solitons. The multiscale spatiotemporal coupling inherent in these systems imposes severe computational bottlenecks on classical high-fidelity numerical simulations. While quantum computing offers the potential for exponential speedup, its unitary dynamics pose a fundamental challenge to solve the NLSE. We propose a quantum framework based on the Lax-pair scattering for solving the 1D NLSE. Specifically, the physical field is first mapped into the spectral space via a quantum direct scattering circuit. Following a decoupled linear time evolution, the physical solution is reconstructed through an inverse scattering transform utilizing the quantum singular value transformation. Since the temporal evolution is performed analytically in the scattering domain, the framework bypasses iterative time stepping, rendering it highly advantageous for long-time simulations. To demonstrate the accuracy and noise resilience of this approach, we simulate a Gaussian wave packet under quantum noise, two-soliton collisions, breather dynamics, and modulational instability on a quantum emulator.


---


## 在纳米石墨烯旋转链中学习非齐次海森堡Hamilton学派

**Original Title:** Learning Inhomogeneous Heisenberg Hamiltonians in Nanographene Spin Chains

**Authors:** Greta Lupi, Saketh Ravuri, Chenxiao Zhao, Weidan Zhang, Cesare Roncaglia, Renxiang Liu, Xinliang Feng, Daniele Passerone, Pascal Ruffieux, Roman Fasel, Jose L. Lado, Gonçalo Catarina

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29281v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29281v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

从实验数据推断微观Hamilton是量子材料和量子模拟的核心挑战。在低维旋转系统中，交换相互作用通常被认为是空间均匀的，尽管结构和环境的不均匀性可以局部改变耦合。在这里，我们利用局部、与长度无关的机器学习方法来直接从非弹性扫描隧道光谱图重建空间调制交换相互作用。我们用纳米石墨烯旋转链展示了这种方法，识别了合成磁铁上的接近均匀和不均匀状态。重建的模型定量地再现了实验光谱，并恢复了激发间隙随系统大小的正确缩放。我们的结果建立了一种通用策略，将局部光谱测量与有效的多体汉密尔顿方程联系起来。


### Abstract

Inferring microscopic Hamiltonians from experimental data is a central challenge in quantum materials and quantum simulation. In low-dimensional spin systems, exchange interactions are often assumed to be spatially uniform, despite structural and environmental inhomogeneities that can locally modify the coupling. Here, we leverage a local, length-independent machine learning methodology to reconstruct spatially modulated exchange interactions directly from inelastic scanning tunneling spectroscopy maps. We demonstrate this approach with nanographene spin chains, identifying both near-uniform and inhomogeneous regimes across the synthesized magnets. The reconstructed models quantitatively reproduce the experimental spectra and recover the correct scaling of the excitation gap with system size. Our results establish a general strategy to bridge local spectroscopic measurements with effective many-body Hamiltonians.


---


## 量子机器学习私人培训

**Original Title:** Private training in quantum machine learning

**Authors:** Tigran Sedrakyan, Frédéric Grosshans, Elham Kashefi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29293v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29293v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

随着在包含潜在敏感数据的大型数据集上训练的机器学习（ML）模型的出现，人工智能安全性的一个主要问题是如何使学习针对训练数据私有化。与经典机器学习类似，量子机器学习（QML）模型并非没有隐私漏洞。差异隐私（DP）是在敏感数据上训练ML模型的标准工具，但其对QML的影响仍然知之甚少。在这项工作中，我们研究了混合变分QML模型中的私人训练，使用应用于具有经典输入和输出的管道的经典私人DP-BCD优化器。我们分析了DP-BCD中梯度限幅和校准噪音添加之间的相互作用，及其对有噪和无噪量子模型的优化和准确性的影响。我们首先解释为什么量子噪音不能为DP-BCD中的校准噪音提供令人满意的替代品以确保隐私。然后，我们展示了一类量子模型的梯度规范的确定性界限如何转化为对DP-BCD引入的有害限幅偏差的显式控制。最后，我们制定了固定限幅阈值和隐私预算下的数字比较协议，并在等效量子和经典模型的合成和图像分类任务中对其进行评估。我们的结果表明，量子模型可以在私人训练机制中保持更高的准确性，其中正式的隐私保证由经典的DP-BCD机制确保。


### Abstract

With the emergence of machine learning (ML) models trained on large datasets containing potentially sensitive data, a major question in AI safety is how to make learning private with respect to the training data. Similar to classical machine learning, quantum machine learning (QML) models are not devoid of privacy vulnerabilities. Differential privacy (DP) is a standard tool for training ML models on sensitive data, but its impact in QML remains poorly understood. In this work we study private training in hybrid variational QML models using a classical private DP-SGD optimizer applied to pipelines with classical inputs and outputs. We analyze the interplay between gradient clipping and calibrated noise addition in DP-SGD, and its impact on optimization and accuracy for noisy and noiseless quantum models. We first explain why quantum noise does not provide a satisfactory replacement for the calibrated noise in DP-SGD for ensuring privacy. We then show how the deterministic bounds on gradient norms for a wide class of quantum models translate into explicit control of the detrimental clipping bias introduced by DP-SGD. Finally, we formulate a numerical comparison protocol under fixed clipping threshold and privacy budget and evaluate it on synthetic and image-classification tasks for equivalent quantum and classical models. Our results suggest that quantum models can retain higher accuracy in private-training regimes where the formal privacy guarantee is ensured by a classical DP-SGD mechanism.


---


## 随机图费米系统中的体积定律和纠缠态的普遍性

**Original Title:** Volume Law and Universality of Entanglement Entropy in Random Graph Fermi Systems

**Authors:** Saikat Sur

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29304v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29304v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

我们研究了Erdspirs-Rényi随机图上自由费米子的底态纠缠论，其中每个可能的边都以一定的概率独立存在。利用随机矩阵理论和渐进自由度，我们证明了在热力学极限下，态纠缠量服从精确的体积定律。纠缠密度，其普适系数独立于边缘概率和图形的微观细节。该系数经过数字确认，以获得约0.386美元$ nats的值，严格低于Page值。因此，体积定律反映了随机图中不存在几何局部性。


### Abstract

We study the ground-state entanglement entropy of free fermions on the Erdős--Rényi random graph, where each of the possible edges is present independently with some probability. Using random matrix theory and asymptotic freeness, we prove that the ground-state entanglement entropy obeys an exact volume law in the thermodynamic limit. The entanglement density, with a universal coefficient that is independent of the edge probability and the microscopic details of the graph. This coefficient is confirmed numerically to take the value approximately $0.386$ nats, strictly below the Page value. The volume law therefore reflects the absence of geometric locality in the random graph.


---


## 物质的伪信息量和拓扑相

**Original Title:** Pseudo entropy and topological phases of matter

**Authors:** Pramod Kamal Kharel, Manghang Limbu, Nabaraj Khatri, Ashish Khanal, Kiran Adhikari

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29311v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29311v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

纠缠论已被证明是对量子混乱和相转变等现象的有力探索。伪熵是最近提出的纠缠度量的类时推广，其动机是德西特全息学。在这项工作中，我们发现伪信息量还可以作为区分物质拓扑相的新探测器。为此，我们将Su--Schrieffer--Heeger模型作为代表性例子，并研究了整个从topical到平凡和平凡到topical的转变中的平均超额熵$ΔS_{12}$，定义为伪信息和平均纠缠信息之间的差。当两个状态处于同相时，我们发现$ ΔS_{12}$在周期性边界条件下是非正的，而对于开放边界条件，只有当系统足够大时它才是非正的。此外，我们还分析了用于跨域猝灭的接地状态猝灭协议，并发现虚伪熵跟踪费舍尔零点预测的临界时间。


### Abstract

Entanglement entropy has proven to be a powerful probe of phenomena such as quantum chaos and phase transitions. Pseudo entropy is a recently proposed time-like generalization of an entanglement measure, motivated by de Sitter holography. In this work, we find that pseudo entropy can also serve as a novel probe for distinguishing topological phases of matter. For this, we consider the Su--Schrieffer--Heeger model as a representative example and investigate the averaged excess entropy $ΔS_{12}$, defined as the difference between pseudo entropy and the average entanglement entropy, across the topological-to-trivial and trivial-to-topological phase transitions. When the two states are in the same phase, we find that $ ΔS_{12}$ is non-positive under periodic boundary conditions, while for open boundary conditions, it is non-positive only when the system is sufficiently large. Moreover, we analyze ground-state quench protocols for topology-crossing quenches and find that the imaginary pseudo entropy tracks the critical times predicted by the Fisher zeros.


---


## 相同粒子的内在不可分割性以及粒子标签如何影响它

**Original Title:** Intrinsic Indistinguishability of Identical Particles and How Particle Labels Affect It

**Authors:** Valery Shchesnovich

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29312v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29312v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

我们研究相同玻色子和费米子经历其可见自由度的任意粒子数保持进化时的不相容性。对于由可见状态投影到对称/反对称子空间上定义的投射不可分割性度量，我们根据动态不变内部状态推导出等效表达。我们通过根据编码动态不变量的不相容性函数推导出多粒子可见状态的显式重建公式，进一步将玻色子和费米子的教科书对称化/反对称化框架推广到任意部分互换性。我们通过广义对称性上的投射度量给出了不可分割类函数的完整刻画。最后，我们揭示了一个明显违反直觉的效果：引入额外的粒子标签状态可以增加相同粒子的多粒子不可混淆性。该效应源于集体多粒子相的抵消。


### Abstract

We investigate indistinguishability of identical bosons and fermions undergoing arbitrary particle-number-preserving evolutions of their visible degrees of freedom. For the projective indistinguishability measure, defined by the projection of the visible state onto the symmetric/anti-symmetric subspace, we derive an equivalent expression in terms of the dynamically invariant internal state. We further generalize the textbook symmetrization/anti-symmetrization framework for bosons and fermions to arbitrary partial distinguishability by deriving an explicit reconstruction formula for the multiparticle visible state in terms of the indistinguishability function encoding the dynamical invariants. We give complete characterization of the class-functions of indistinguishability by projective measures on generalized symmetries. Finally, we reveal a strikingly counterintuitive effect: introducing additional particle label states can increase the multiparticle indistinguishability of identical particles. The effect originates from the cancellation of collective multiparticle phases.


---


## 具有相对运动的磁量系统中的涌现能量尺度

**Original Title:** Emergent energy scales in magnonic systems with relative motion

**Authors:** Daigo Oue

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29316v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29316v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

相互作用的系统之间的相对运动可以产生孤立系统中所不存在的新兴能量尺度。虽然单色运动可以通过伽利略变换消除，但相互作用系统之间的相对运动通常不能。在存在特征空间结构的情况下，相对运动会产生由激励的特征波矢和系统的相对速度确定的多普勒频率标度。这种新兴规模为驱动运动系统中的非平衡现象提供了基本机制。特别地，涌现能量尺度由相对运动如何探测相关激发的空间结构来确定。在本教程中，我们使用magnonic系统作为具体平台来说明这些想法。我们首先讨论相对运动的铁磁体之间的运动诱导的磁振子输运，其中多普勒频率作为一个有效的非平衡偏置的微扰制度。这种机制甚至在没有常规驱动力（如温度梯度或化学势差）的情况下也会产生磁振子电流。然后我们引入运动引起的参数不稳定性。当涌现的尺度变得足够大以共振地产生磁振子对时，微扰描述就会崩溃，磁振子真空就会变得不稳定。在临界速度阈值以上，自发产生磁振子对，导致输运和非平衡动力学强烈增强。还强调了与相关现象的联系，包括量子摩擦、切伦科夫发射和泽尔多维奇超辐射。新兴能量尺度的概念为理解具有相对运动的量子系统中的输运现象和不稳定性提供了一个统一的框架。


### Abstract

Relative motion between interacting systems can generate emergent energy scales that are absent in isolated systems. While uniform motion can be eliminated by a Galilean transformation, relative motion between interacting systems generally cannot. In the presence of characteristic spatial structures, relative motion gives rise to a Doppler frequency scale determined by the characteristic wavevector of the excitation and the relative velocity of the system. This emergent scale provides a fundamental mechanism for driving nonequilibrium phenomena in moving systems. In particular, the emergent energy scale is determined by how the relative motion probes the spatial structure of the relevant excitation. In this tutorial, we illustrate these ideas using magnonic systems as a concrete platform. We first discuss motion-induced magnon transport between relatively moving ferromagnets, in which the Doppler frequency serves as an effective nonequilibrium bias in the perturbative regime. This mechanism produces magnon currents even in the absence of conventional driving forces such as temperature gradients or chemical potential differences. We then introduce motion-induced parametric instabilities. When the emergent scale becomes sufficiently large to resonantly create magnon pairs, the perturbative description breaks down, and the magnonic vacuum becomes unstable. Above a critical velocity threshold, spontaneous magnon-pair creation emerges, resulting in strongly enhanced transport and nonequilibrium dynamics. Connections to related phenomena, including quantum friction, Cherenkov emission, and Zeldovich superradiance, are also highlighted. The concept of an emergent energy scale provides a unifying framework for understanding transport phenomena and instabilities in quantum systems with relative motion.


---


## 零记忆量子点水库计算的几何方法

**Original Title:** Geometric Approach to Zero-Memory Quantum Dot Reservoir Computing

**Authors:** Bongsu Kim, Oscar Lee, Sangjun Jeon, Kun Woo Kim

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29320v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29320v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

物理储层计算为传统神经网络提供了一种节能替代方案，其中物理系统中的固有记忆容量发挥着核心作用。我们证明，通过利用计算时空权衡，用空间自由度取代时间记忆，可以在无记忆系统中对存储容量进行外部设计。我们的方法利用多维输入节点作为空间记忆轴，从而消除了对水库中固有的历史相关动态的依赖。我们通过对广义量子点的数值模拟来验证这一框架，其离散能量水平也提供了对储层计算至关重要的强非线性。通过将这种固有的非线性与我们的外部记忆相结合，我们表明无记忆量子库可以在混乱的麦基-格拉斯未来预测和非线性转换任务中实现高性能。此外，通过分析量子状态轨迹的几何形状，我们确定了这种记忆出现背后的物理机制：外部记忆在量子希尔伯特空间内构建了一个滞后环，当系统状态的演变与输入信号的频率同步时，这个环变得拓扑稳定。我们的工作将库计算与特定材料的存储属性分开，显着扩大了量子神经形态计算候选系统的范围。


### Abstract

Physical reservoir computing offers an energy-efficient alternative to conventional neural networks, where the intrinsic memory capacity in the physical system plays a central role. We demonstrate that memory capacity can be engineered extrinsically in memoryless systems by exploiting the computational space-time tradeoff, substituting temporal memory with spatial degrees of freedom. Our approach utilizes multidimensional input nodes to function as a spatial memory axis, thereby removing the dependency on intrinsic history-dependent dynamics in the reservoir. We validate this framework through numerical simulations of a generalized quantum dot, whose discrete energy levels provide strong nonlinearity crucial for reservoir computing as well. By coupling this inherent nonlinearity with our extrinsic memory, we show that memoryless quantum reservoir can achieve high performance on both chaotic Mackey-Glass future prediction and nonlinear transformation tasks. Furthermore, by analyzing the geometry of the quantum state trajectories, we identify the physical mechanism underlying this memory emergence: extrinsic memory constructs a hysteresis loop within the quantum Hilbert space, and this loop becomes topologically stable when the evolution of the system state synchronizes with the input signal's frequency. Our work decouples reservoir computing from material-specific memory properties, significantly expanding the range of candidate systems for quantum neuromorphic computing.


---


## 伪随机状态的通用副本数放大

**Original Title:** Generic Number-of-Copies Amplification for Pseudorandom States

**Authors:** Zvika Brakerski, Miri Zenilman

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29325v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29325v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

我们表明，对于安全参数中的任何多项$t$，任何针对单副本加密器安全的量子伪随机状态（即$1$-PPA）都可以被放大到$t $-Copy安全性（即$t$-PPA），无需额外假设。之前的工作（Ananth和Goldin，arXiv 2025）只能证明有限类别的1美元-PRS结构，即其生成器仅使用少量辅助量子位的结构。从技术上讲，我们表明，通过仔细考虑构造中使用的随机性并使用量子提取器，可以消除任何长度的辅助寄存器并获得有意义的$t$-SES结果。


### Abstract

We show that any quantum pseudorandom state that is secure against single-copy distinguishers, i.e. a $1$-PRS, can be amplified to $t$-copy security, i.e. to a $t$-PRS, without additional assumptions, for any polynomial $t$ in the security parameter. Prior work (Ananth and Goldin, arXiv 2025) was only able to show this for a restricted class of $1$-PRS constructions, namely ones whose generators only use a small number of ancilla qubits. Technically, we show that by carefully accounting for the randomness that is used in the construction, and using quantum extractors, it is possible to eliminate an ancilla register of any length and obtain a meaningful $t$-PRS outcome.


---


## 偶极量子气体中量子液滴的呼吸模式：求和规则分析

**Original Title:** Breathing mode of quantum droplets in dipolar quantum gases: A sum-rule analysis

**Authors:** Xinran Zhang, Junli Liu, Huiyun Xiao, Xiao-Long Chen, Yunbo Zhang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29370v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29370v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

我们从理论上研究了包含量子涨落的各向异性谐振陷阱中三维偶极玻色气体的接地特性和呼吸模式集体激发。将高斯变分分析与非微扰总和规则分析相结合，我们推导出轴向和放射呼吸模式频率的显式解析表达，并通过与时相关的扩展Gross-Pitaevskii方程的数值解进行了验证。我们的理论预测表明，与$^{166}$Eu和$^{162}$Dyy气体的现有实验数据非常一致。通过在$s$-波散射长度、原子数和陷阱长宽比的参数空间构建全面的相图，我们揭示了稀玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚相和稠密量子液滴相之间的不连续一级相转变和光滑交叉。我们证实，与传统的弱相互作用玻色气体相比，量子涨落引起的增强的不可压缩性显着提高了液滴相的呼吸模式频率。此外，该系统在准二维和准一维约束下在散射长度上经历了相转变和交叉，其特征分别是峰值密度和原子云尺寸的不连续跳跃和连续交叉。我们的工作提供了一个严格且高度准确的框架来描述偶极量子气体中的集体激发，为即将到来的稀土元素原子和极分子超冷原子实验提供了定量见解。


### Abstract

We theoretically investigate the ground-state properties and breathing-mode collective excitations of three-dimensional dipolar Bose gases in anisotropic harmonic traps incorporating quantum fluctuations. Combining a Gaussian variational ansatz with a non-perturbative sum-rule analysis, we derive explicit analytical expressions for both axial and radial breathing-mode frequencies, which are validated by numerical solutions of the time-dependent extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation. Our theoretical predictions show excellent agreement with existing experimental data for $^{166}$Er and $^{162}$Dy gases. By constructing comprehensive phase diagrams across the parameter space of the $s$-wave scattering length, atom number, and trap aspect ratio, we reveal both discontinuous first-order phase transitions and smooth crossovers between the dilute Bose-Einstein condensate and dense quantum droplet phases. We confirm that the enhanced incompressibility induced by quantum fluctuations significantly elevates the breathing-mode frequencies in the droplet phase compared to conventional weakly interacting Bose gases. Furthermore, the system undergoes a phase transition and a crossover over the scattering length under the quasi-two-dimensional and quasi-one-dimensional confinements, characterized by discontinuous jumps and continuous crossovers in peak density and atomic cloud sizes, respectively. Our work offers a rigorous and highly accurate framework to characterize collective excitations in dipolar quantum gases, providing quantitative insights for forthcoming ultracold atom experiments in lanthanide atoms and polar molecules.


---


## 人类首次量子纠缠成像

**Original Title:** First-in-human quantum entanglement imaging

**Authors:** Pawel Moskal, Deepak Kumar, Sushil Sharma, Ermias Y. Beyene, Neha Chug, Catalina Curceanu, Eryk Czerwiński, Atharva Dalvi, Manish Das, Alicja Hubalewska-Dydejczyk, Sharareh Jalali, Krzysztof Kacprzak, Tevfik Kaplanoglu, Łukasz Kapłon, Kamila Kasperska, Aleksander Khreptak, Grzegorz Korcyl, Tomasz Kozik, Sumit Kumar Kundu, Anoop Kunimmal Venadan, Bartosz Leszczyński, Edward Lisowski, Filip Lisowski, Justyna Mędrala-Sowa, Simbarashe Moyo, Wiktor Mryka, Szymon Niedźwiecki, Marta Opalińska, Anand Pandey, Piyush Pandey, Alessio Porcelli, Bartłomiej Rachwał, Magdalena Skurzok, Anna Sowa-Staszczak, Tomasz Szumlak, Satyam Tiwari, Pooja Tanty, Keyvan Tayefi Ardebili, Kavya Valsan Eliyan, Ewa Ł. Stepień

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29421v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29421v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

湮灭光子在偏振中是量子纠缠的，这是一种迄今为止尚未在医学诊断中利用的现象。我们提出了第一次在体内成像的量子纠缠的光子起源于正电子-电子湮灭的程度在人类受试者。本研究使用Jagiellonian正电子发射断层扫描（J-PET）扫描仪，由塑料制造。在塑料中，湮灭光子主要通过康普顿效应相互作用，康普顿效应提供了关于光子相互作用位置和时间以及光子偏振平面的同时信息。该患者注射了标有$^{68}$Ga放射性核素的DOTA-TATE放射性药物。使用J-PET扫描仪，我们确定了放射性药物吸收的图像，同时确定了量子纠缠度的图像。后者是根据湮没量子的极化平面之间的相对角度确定的。为肝脏和脾脏提取的量子纠缠度值小于对最大纠缠双量子状态的预测值，但大于对可分离量子的预期值。该演示为量子纠缠在临床诊断中的应用开辟了新的视角。


### Abstract

Annihilation photons are quantum-entangled in polarization, a phenomenon that has not been exploited in medical diagnostics so far. We present the first in vivo imaging of the degree of quantum entanglement of photons originating from positron-electron annihilation within a human subject. This study utilized the Jagiellonian Positron Emission Tomography (J-PET) scanner, constructed from plastic scintillators. In plastics, annihilation photons interact primarily via the Compton effect, which provides simultaneous information regarding the photon interaction position and time, as well as the photon polarization plane. The patient was injected with a DOTA-TATE radiopharmaceutical labeled with the $^{68}$Ga radionuclide. Using the J-PET scanner, we determined the image of the radiopharmaceutical uptake and, simultaneously, the image of the degree of quantum entanglement. The latter was determined from the relative angle between the polarization planes of the annihilation photons. The values of the degree of quantum entanglement extracted for the liver and the spleen are smaller than those predicted for maximally entangled two-photon states, yet larger than expected for separable photons. This demonstration opens new perspectives for the application of quantum entanglement in clinical diagnostics.


---


## 挤压增强的压缩增强成对聚变

**Original Title:** Squeezing-enhanced Pairwise Fusion of Photonic Qudits

**Authors:** Pradip Laha, Peter van Loock

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29432v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29432v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

成对聚变门是线性光学测量，预示着贝尔投影到两个d轨单量子量子的两轨子空间上。在没有辅助输入量子的情况下，这些被动测量以概率\（1-d^{-1}\）成功，所有失败仅限于对角逻辑子空间。我们表明，在子数解析检测恢复该结构性故障部分之前，将相同的单一模式压缩器应用于\（2d）干涉仪输出。光数宇称保留了成功的非对角线融合特征，而选择的全偶数图案产生与确定的成对贝尔投影仪成比例的POVM元素。我们推导出精确的逻辑空间POVM，并证明对角线图案被接受当且仅当其光数失衡载体恰好具有两个大小相等的非零分量。由此产生的闭椭圆积分表达增加了理想的成功概率，例如，对于\（d=4\），从\（75%\）增加到\（79.62%\），对于\（d=6\），从\（83.33%\）增加到\（87.15%\）。对于代表性的有限检测器饱和阈值，\（n_{\rm sat}=7\），相应的认证值保持\（78.84\%\）和\（86.71\%\）。这些结果确立了主动高斯处理作为一种在没有辅助输入量子的情况下回收结构化测量失败的方法，其代价是\（2d\）压缩操作和检测时更大的量子数范围。


### Abstract

Pairwise fusion gates are linear-optical measurements that herald Bell projections onto two-rail subspaces of two \(d\)-rail single-photon qudits. Without ancillary input photons, these passive measurements succeed with probability \(1-d^{-1}\), with all failures confined to the diagonal logical subspace. We show that identical single-mode squeezers applied to the \(2d\) interferometer outputs before photon-number-resolving detection recover part of this structured failure sector. Photon-number parity preserves the successful off-diagonal fusion signatures, while selected all-even patterns yield POVM elements proportional to definite pairwise Bell projectors. We derive the exact logical-space POVM and prove that a diagonal pattern is accepted if and only if its photon-number-imbalance vector has exactly two nonzero components of equal magnitude. The resulting closed elliptic-integral expression increases the ideal success probability, for instance, from \(75\%\) to \(79.62\%\) for \(d=4\), and from \(83.33\%\) to \(87.15\%\) for \(d=6\). With a representative finite detector saturation threshold, \(n_{\rm sat}=7\), the respective certified values remain \(78.84\%\) and \(86.71\%\). These results establish active Gaussian processing as a method for recycling structured measurement failures without ancillary input photons, at the cost of \(2d\) squeezing operations and a larger photon-number range at detection.


---


## 自主量子热机中的稳态贝尔非定域性

**Original Title:** Steady-state Bell nonlocality in an autonomous quantum thermal machine

**Authors:** Bradley Longstaff

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29434v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29434v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

提出了一种能够自主产生稳态贝尔非定域性的量子热机。为两个不连贯地耦合到一对热浴的量子比特推导出Lindblad方程，并发现由此产生的刘维利安具有很强的对称性。对于某些初始条件，这个失平衡系统可以在一系列参数和任意高温下产生Bell非局部稳态。为了分析机器如何在更现实的环境中运行，然后通过对系统汉密尔顿量的随机扰动将实验缺陷纳入其中。这打破了强对称性，并导致集体和局部去相噪音。研究发现，如果唯一的噪音源是局部噪音，那么稳态是贝尔局部。集体噪音的共存被证明是有利的，能够增加贝尔不等式违反的程度，并将稳态从贝尔局部转换为贝尔非局部。


### Abstract

A quantum thermal machine is presented that is able to autonomously generate steady-state Bell nonlocality. A Lindblad equation is derived for two qubits that are incoherently coupled to a pair of thermal baths and the resulting Liouvillian is found to have a strong symmetry. This out-of-equilibrium system can generate Bell-nonlocal steady states across a range of parameters and at arbitrarily high temperatures for certain initial conditions. To analyse how the machine operates in a more realistic setting, experimental imperfections are then included via a stochastic perturbation to the system Hamiltonian. This breaks the strong symmetry and results in collective and local dephasing noise. It is found that if the sole source of noise is local noise, then the steady state is Bell local. The co-presence of collective noise is then shown to be advantageous, with the ability to increase the degree of Bell-inequality violation and transform a steady state from Bell local to Bell nonlocal.


---


## 稳定器信息对于混合状态是值得信赖的

**Original Title:** Stabilizer entropy is trustworthy for mixed states

**Authors:** Gianluca Esposito, Michele Viscardi, Alioscia Hamma

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29443v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29443v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

事实证明，量化混合状态中的非稳定性是很困难的，因为任何严格的单调都需要超指数时间。我们提出了一种线性稳定器熵，当限制于作用于平坦混合稳定器状态的非自适应Clifford通道时，它以压倒性的概率充当适当的非稳定性单调。哈尔随机状态、克利福德轨道和随机矩阵积状态的分析和数值结果表明，单调性违背概率衰减为$\BEP-n$。我们还证明了稳定器信息在接受部分测量的特定多体系统中的有效性，其中每个测量结果的资源量以及结果概率的平均值都不会增加。考虑到严格替代方案的难度，稳定器熵成为一种实用且理论上合理的资源衡量标准。


### Abstract

Quantifying non-stabilizerness in mixed states is provably intractable, as any strict monotone requires superexponential time. We propose a linear Stabilizer Entropy that acts as a proper non-stabilizerness monotone with overwhelming probability when restricted to non-adaptive Clifford channels acting on flat mixed stabilizer states. Analytical and numerical results for Haar-random states, Clifford orbits, and random matrix product states show that monotonicity violation probabilities decay as $\exp-ηN$. We also prove the validity of Stabilizer Entropy in specific many-body systems undergoing partial measurements, where the amount of resource never increases for each measurement outcome as well as when averaged over outcome probabilities. Given the hardness of strict alternatives, Stabilizer Entropy emerges as a practical and theoretically justified resource measure.


---


## 超越量子位极限的超量子量子链接

**Original Title:** A superconducting qutrit link beyond the qubit limit

**Authors:** Xiang Li, Zheng-Yang Mei, Yang He, Si-Lu Zhao, Yan-Jun Liu, Xiao-Hui Song, Kai Xu, Zhong-Cheng Xiang, Dong-Ning Zheng, Heng Fan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29475v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29475v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

超导微波链路已经实现了量子位之间的确定性状态转移和远程纠缠，但迄今为止，确定性链路一直在有效的二维传输希尔伯特空间中运行。在这里，我们演示了通过微波通道连接的两个独立封装的节点之间的一个超导链接。每个节点结合了一个transmon qutrit、一个传输共振器和一个可调Purcell-过滤器接口，允许两个远程微波-量子接口在频率和带宽上匹配。我们实现了两个转变选择性光介导的操作，以转移$|e\rangle$和$|f\rangle$quutrit分量处于同一通道的不同时间模式。我们以断层扫描方式描述了任意四进制状态转移，获得了83.68%的平均转移状态保真度和77.12%的四进制处理保真度，超过了经典四进制转移基准和用于传输任意四进制比特的有效量子位通道的最佳可能平均保真度。使用部分转移操作，我们重建了负性0.730的远程二进制状态，断层摄影推断的密集编码容量为2.273位，断层摄影推断的Collins-Gisin-Linden-Massar-Popescu（CGLMP）参数$I_3=2.332$，所有这些都超出了相应的量子位或局部边界。这些结果证明了一种使用Transmons的原生三级结构作为真正的多维通信资源的超导微波链路。


### Abstract

Superconducting microwave links have enabled deterministic state transfer and remote entanglement between qubits, but deterministic links have so far operated with an effectively two-dimensional transmitted Hilbert space. Here we demonstrate a superconducting qutrit link between two independently packaged nodes connected by a microwave channel. Each node combines a transmon qutrit, a transmission resonator, and a tunable Purcell-filter interface, allowing the two remote microwave-photon interfaces to be matched in both frequency and bandwidth. We implement two transition-selective photon-mediated operations that transfer the $|e\rangle$ and $|f\rangle$ qutrit components in distinct temporal modes of the same channel. We tomographically characterize arbitrary qutrit-state transfer, obtaining a mean transferred-state fidelity of 83.68% and a qutrit process fidelity of 77.12%, exceeding both the classical qutrit-transfer benchmark and the best possible average fidelity of an effective qubit channel used to transmit an arbitrary qutrit. Using partial-transfer operations, we reconstruct a remote two-qutrit state with negativity 0.730, a tomography-inferred dense-coding capacity of 2.273 bits, and a tomography-inferred Collins-Gisin-Linden-Massar-Popescu (CGLMP) parameter $I_3=2.332$, all beyond the corresponding qubit or local bounds. These results demonstrate a superconducting microwave link that uses the native three-level structure of transmons as a genuine high-dimensional communication resource.


---


## 多维赤道上量子态的测量集中现象

**Original Title:** Concentration of Measure Phenomena for Quantum States on a Higher Dimensional Equator

**Authors:** Kabgyun Jeong

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29487v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29487v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

我们重温莱维引理，这是量子信息理论中广泛使用的分析工具。集中不平等量化了利普希茨可观测量集中在中位数或平均值附近的现象，并充当信息论、统计物理和学习理论的基本分析工具。特别是，莱维引理为描述纯量子状态的函式提供了一个重要框架，并在量子纠缠和量子统计查询学习中应用。在这项工作中，我们分离了标准球浓度论点的超赤道部分。所得估计是Lipschitz函数在固定超方程上的Lévy型界，自然维数参数为$d-1$。我们还制定了相应的几何本地化的边界，hyperequator，和一个codimension-two antipodal大子球的邻域。这一观点阐明了通常的证明结构，并指出了更清晰的常数级陈述所需的测度论公式。


### Abstract

We revisit Lévy's lemma, a widely used analytical tool in quantum information theory. Concentration inequalities quantify the phenomenon in which Lipschitz observables concentrate around a median or mean, and serve as fundamental analytical tools across information theory, statistical physics, and learning theory. In particular, Lévy's lemma provides a crucial framework for describing functionals on pure quantum states, with applications in quantum entanglement and quantum statistical query learning. In this work, we isolate the hyper-equatorial part of the standard spherical concentration argument. The resulting estimate is a Lévy-type bound for Lipschitz functions on a fixed hyperequator, with the natural dimension parameter $d-1$. We also formulate the accompanying geometric localization in terms of neighborhoods of the boundary, hyperequator, and a codimension-two antipodal great subsphere. This viewpoint clarifies the structure of the usual proof and points to the measure-theoretic formulation needed for sharper constant-level statements.


---


## 使用TEPID-ADAPT-VQE算法量子模拟分子激发态流和能量

**Original Title:** Quantum simulation of molecular excited-state manifolds and energies using the TEPID-ADAPT-VQE algorithm

**Authors:** Jason Saroni, Bharath Sambasivam, Ayush Asthana, Edwin Barnes

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29547v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29547v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

分子激发态的模拟是量子化学的一个关键挑战，也是量子计算的一个有前途的应用。在这项工作中，我们研究了截断特征值参数化初始密度自适应变分算法（TEPID-ADAPT-VQE）计算低位激发态和势能面的有效性。TEPID-ADAPT可变地对角化截短的低温吉布斯态，从而能够在单次优化中同时制备多个激发态。我们将该方法应用于跨越弱相关和强相关区域的键长的H$_2$、LiH和线性H$_4$。自适应求导组装问题定制（ADAPT）类比结构产生了适合短期硬件的紧凑电路。我们还实现了MORE-ADAPT-VQE算法的修改版本，以与TEPID-ADAPT进行比较。我们发现，这两种算法都可以在化学准确度内准确地重现所研究的所有分子和几何形状的激发态光谱和动能曲线。然而，TEPID-ADAPT的优点是仅利用单个物理激励超参数（温度），该超参数控制激发态所针对的能量尺度，而MORE-ADAPT利用多个超参数，其最佳值敏感地取决于目标问题。这些结果表明，结合自适应animals建设与密度矩阵为基础的配方提供了一个有效的框架，激发态量子化学的近期设备。


### Abstract

The simulation of molecular excited states is a key challenge in quantum chemistry and a promising application for quantum computing. In this work, we investigate the efficacy of the truncated eigenvalue parametrized initial density adaptive variational algorithm (TEPID-ADAPT-VQE) for computing low-lying excited states and potential energy surfaces. TEPID-ADAPT variationally diagonalizes a truncated low-temperature Gibbs state, enabling the simultaneous preparation of multiple excited states within a single optimization. We apply the method to H$_2$, LiH, and linear H$_4$ across bond lengths spanning weakly and strongly correlated regimes. The adaptive derivative-assembled problem-tailored (ADAPT) ansatz construction yields compact circuits suitable for near-term hardware. We also implement a modified version of the MORE-ADAPT-VQE algorithm for comparison with TEPID-ADAPT. We find that both algorithms accurately reproduce excited-state spectra and potential energy curves within chemical accuracy for all the molecules and geometries studied. However, TEPID-ADAPT has the advantage of utilizing only a single, physically motivated hyperparameter (temperature) that controls the energy scale at which excited states are targeted, while MORE-ADAPT utilizes multiple hyperparameters whose optimal values depend sensitively on the target problem. These results demonstrate that combining adaptive ansatz construction with density-matrix-based formulations provides an efficient framework for excited-state quantum chemistry on near-term devices.


---


## 纳米空隙作为硅中动量工程光电子学的光学天线

**Original Title:** Nanometric voids as optical antennas for rewritable momentum-engineered photonics in silicon

**Authors:** Aleksei I. Noskov, Evan P. Garcia, Haiping Sun, Eric O. Potma, Dmitry A. Fishman

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29551v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29551v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

光学天线被广泛用于将电磁场定位在远低于折射极限的地方，从而增强纳米光与物质的相互作用。然而，光学约束接近固体中电子德布罗意波长的制度（其中，量子动量分布充分拓宽以放宽光学选择规则）在很大程度上仍然没有被探索。在这里，我们表明嵌入晶体硅中的纳米空隙充当此类光学天线，在不引入任何异物的情况下显着改变间接半导体的光学响应。使用电诱导熔冷过程，我们在整个体硅中产生了纳米空隙，这通过高分辨率电子显微镜、折射分析、傅里叶过滤网格重建、元素映射来证实，并得到光学和振动光谱的支持。含空隙的硅表现出强烈的宽带光致发光和电致发光，在光谱上与相似尺寸的金属或半导体纳米限制器产生的光致发光没有区别，这表明介电不连续性，而不是限制器组成，决定了观察到的动量辅助光学转变。发光可以通过交替的电调节和光学重结晶重复写入、擦除和重写。这些发现将纳米空隙确立为以前未探索的极端光学限制平台，并证明了光学功能可以直接嵌入和重新配置在体硅中。


### Abstract

Optical antennas are widely used to localize electromagnetic fields far below the diffraction limit, enabling enhanced light-matter interactions across nanophotonics. Yet the regime in which optical confinement approaches the electronic de Broglie wavelength in a solid - where the photon momentum distribution broadens sufficiently to relax optical selection rules - remains largely unexplored. Here we show that nanometric voids embedded within crystalline silicon act as such optical antennas, dramatically altering the optical response of an indirect semiconductor without the introduction of any foreign material. Using an electrically induced melt-quench process, we generate nanometric voids throughout bulk silicon, confirmed by high-resolution electron microscopy, diffraction analysis, Fourier-filtered lattice reconstruction, elemental mapping, and supported by optical and vibrational spectroscopies. The void-containing silicon exhibits intense broadband photo- and electroluminescence spectrally indistinguishable from that produced by metallic or semiconductor nanoconfiners of similar dimensions, establishing that dielectric discontinuity, not confiner composition, governs the observed momentum-assisted optical transitions. The luminescence can be repeatedly written, erased, and rewritten through alternating electrical conditioning and optical recrystallization. These findings establish nanometric voids as a previously unexplored platform for extreme optical confinement and demonstrate that photonic functionality can be embedded and reconfigured directly within bulk silicon.


---


## 持不同意见的QAOA

**Original Title:** The QAOA on the ring of disagrees

**Authors:** Kunal Marwaha

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29562v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29562v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

我们研究在循环图上寻找大切割的对称局部算法的性能。此类无法在深度p处看到整个图的算法在期望中最多切割边缘的（2 p +1）/（2 p +2）部分。我们证明QAOA实现了这一价值，这是法希、戈德斯通和古特曼长期存在的猜测。奇怪的是，我们在没有找到最佳参数的情况下这样做。相反，我们证明了这相当于找到次数最多为2 p-1的最佳洛朗式对。这是通过在量子信号处理语言中将QAOA重新铸造到一个量子位上来实现的。


### Abstract

We study the performance of symmetric local algorithms finding large cuts on the cycle graph. Such algorithms that cannot see the whole graph at depth p cut at most a (2p+1)/(2p+2) fraction of edges in expectation. We prove that the QAOA achieves this value, a long-standing conjecture of Farhi, Goldstone, and Gutmann. Curiously we do this without finding the optimal parameters. Instead we show it is equivalent to find an optimal pair of Laurent polynomials of degree at most 2p-1. This is made possible by recasting the QAOA on one qubit in the language of quantum signal processing.


---


## STEMGym：自主电子显微镜剂量预算下的顺序决策基准

**Original Title:** STEMGym: Benchmarking Sequential Decision-Making under Dose Budgets in Autonomous Electron Microscopy

**Authors:** Can Polat, Erchin Serpedin, Mustafa Kurban, Hasan Kurban

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29592v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29592v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

自主科学成像的一个核心前提是，更智能的导航，无论是基于Bayesian、基于RL的导航还是其他自适应的导航，都是实现样本高效采集的主要杠杆。我们在扫描传输电子显微镜（STEM）中提供了相反的证据，这是一种原子分辨率成像模式，其每次测量都会沉积破坏性的电子剂量。我们引入了STEMGym，这是一个开源的Gymnasium基准，包含15个物理模拟STEM世界，涵盖5种材料、3种难度水平和4种特征任务，通过剂量效率曲线区域（DEC-UC）进行评分，这是一个捕捉信息与剂量帕累托前沿的单一量表。在现实剂量预算下的33种药剂配置中，剂量效率的主要决定因素是分析师（感知）管道，而不是导航员：将训练有素的CNN分析师与天真的格栅扫描配对，将DEC-AUC比无CNN的格栅基线提高5.5倍（0.287 vs.\ 0.052），而用Bayesian或自适应有限状态机导航代替格栅不会产生统计上显着的进一步收益。生产层视觉语言模型在晶体学缺陷分析方面的表现进一步落后于特定任务的CNN 13倍。通过在统一剂量预算下分离感知、导航和规划，STEMGym重新定义了ML工作应投资于自主电子显微镜的地方，并提供了对其进行测试的测量基础设施。


### Abstract

A central premise of autonomous scientific imaging is that smarter navigation, whether Bayesian, RL-based, or otherwise adaptive, is the principal lever for sample-efficient acquisition. We present evidence to the contrary in scanning transmission electron microscopy (STEM), an atomic-resolution imaging modality whose every measurement deposits damaging electron dose. We introduce STEMGym, an open-source Gymnasium benchmark of 15 physics-simulated STEM worlds spanning five materials, three difficulty levels, and four characterisation tasks, scored by the Dose-Efficiency Curve area (DEC-AUC), a single scalar capturing the information-vs-dose Pareto frontier. Across 33 agent configurations under realistic dose budgets, the dominant determinant of dose efficiency is the analyst (perception) pipeline, not the navigator: pairing a trained CNN analyst with naïve raster scanning raises DEC-AUC by 5.5x over a CNN-free raster baseline (0.287 vs.\ 0.052), while substituting Bayesian or adaptive finite-state-machine navigation for raster yields no statistically significant further gain. Production-tier vision-language models further underperform task-specific CNNs by {\sim}13x on crystallographic defect analysis. By decoupling perception, navigation, and planning under a unified dose budget, STEMGym reframes where ML effort should be invested in autonomous electron microscopy and provides the measurement infrastructure to test it.


---


## 莫尔斯分子系统中扩展旋转振动光关联的物理信息神经量子控制

**Original Title:** Physics-Informed Neural Quantum Control for Extended Rovibrational Photoassociation in a Morse Molecular System

**Authors:** Murilo D. Forlevesi, Emanuel Fernandes de Lima, Edson Denis Leonel

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29610v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29610v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

我们提出了一个物理知情神经量子控制（PINQC）框架，用于莫尔斯分子系统中的旋转振动光关联。所提出的方法将基于神经网络的激光场产生与可微量子传播相结合，允许直接从底层量子动力学中获得优化的激光脉冲，而无需外部训练数据。优化的控制场有效地将最初类似连续体的高斯波包转移到振动基态水平，通过连贯旋转振动动力学促进连续体到束缚粒子数转移。由此产生的光关联过程涉及振动稳定化和旋转重新分布，这两个旋转重新分布由相邻旋转通道之间的偶极诱导的耦合自然产生。本工作的一个核心结果是将PINQC框架成功应用于扩展的旋转振动模型，该模型包含比我们以前在传统光关联计算中获得的旋转水平更大的旋转水平。尽管分子系统的复杂性增加，但优化在数值上仍然保持稳定，这表明可微优化为处理维度增加的旋转振动模型提供了有效的策略。这些结果确立了PINQC框架作为分子光关联的一种有前途的计算工具，并激发了未来对日益复杂的旋转振动量子控制问题的研究。


### Abstract

We present a Physics-Informed Neural Quantum Control (PINQC) framework for rovibrational photoassociation in a Morse molecular system. The proposed method combines neural-network-based laser-field generation with differentiable quantum propagation, allowing optimized laser pulses to be obtained directly from the underlying quantum dynamics without requiring external training data. The optimized control fields efficiently transfer an initially continuum-like Gaussian wave packet into the vibrational ground-state level, promoting continuum-to-bound population transfer through coherent rovibrational dynamics. The resulting photoassociation process involves both vibrational stabilization and rotational redistribution arising naturally from dipole-induced couplings between neighboring rotational channels. A central result of the present work is the successful application of the PINQC framework to extended rovibrational models containing larger rotational levels than those previously accessible in our conventional photoassociation calculations. The optimization remains numerically stable despite the increased complexity of the molecular system, demonstrating that differentiable optimization provides an effective strategy for treating rovibrational models of increased dimensionality. These results establish the PINQC framework as a promising computational tool for molecular photoassociation and motivate future investigations of increasingly complex rovibrational quantum-control problems.


---


## 具有现实线性传感器的高斯量子计量学

**Original Title:** Gaussian Quantum Metrology with Realistic Linear Sensors

**Authors:** Jacques Ding, James W. Gardner, Tuvia Gefen, Yanbei Chen

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29616v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29616v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

量子传感有望提高精确度，但通常的量子克莱默·拉奥界限对于现实的线性传感器来说可能过于乐观，因为压缩、过滤和损失重塑了量子噪音。我们推导出了紧Holevo Cramer Rao界限，并表明现实退化会产生具有通常界限和零差读出的层次结构。这种层次结构已经存在于引力波探测器中。我们提出了一种硬件高效的读出，可以在没有额外信号损失的情况下达到Holevo界限，与目前的LIGO零差读出相比，将紧凑二进制检测率提高高达25%。


### Abstract

Quantum sensing promises enhanced precision, but the usual quantum Cramer Rao bound can be too optimistic for realistic linear sensors, where squeezing, filtering, and loss reshape quantum noise. We derive the tight Holevo Cramer Rao bound and show that realistic degradation yields a hierarchy with the usual bound and homodyne readout. This hierarchy already exists in gravitational-wave detectors. We propose a hardware-efficient readout that reaches the Holevo bound without extra signal loss, increasing compact-binary detection rates by up to 25% over the present LIGO homodyne readout.


---


## 两个含时耦合谐振子中量子纠缠的动力学

**Original Title:** Dynamics of quantum entanglement in two time-dependent coupled harmonic oscillators

**Authors:** Ayoub Ghaba, Radouan Hab-arrih, Elhoussine Atmani, Abdallah Slaoui

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29617v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29617v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

我们研究了两个具有含时相互作用的耦合谐振子的量子纠缠动力学。使用Lewis-Riesenfeld不变量方法，我们在没有任何微扰或隔热逼近的情况下推导出精确的分析波函数，并将其与使用Wigner函数的相空间分析相结合，以提供系统量子状态演变的完整描述。对于任意激发数$（n，m）$，我们获得了纯度和线性熵$S_L=1-\mathCal{P}$的一般表达形式，从而可以系统地研究一大类量子态的纠缠。我们表明，纠缠动力学对失调参数$θ$和$\vartheta_2 $、频率参数$β_0$和耦合强度$e $之间的相互作用非常敏感：失调的增加使系统从缓慢的不规则振荡转变为快速和规则的周期行为，更强的耦合系统性地增强了线性熵的幅度和平均值。最重要的是，对于共振情况$ω_1=ω_2=1$和强耦合$δ\大约0.99$，该系统对于所有考虑的量子状态都表现出线性熵的鲁棒无衰减同步周期振荡，这表明保留了量子相干性而没有饱和。我们的研究结果表明，线性熵是一个敏感且实用的纠缠见证，并且我们在系统的耦合参数与其纠缠性质之间建立了显式的分析关系，这些关系与连续变量系统中的量子信息处理和量子相关性的控制直接相关。


### Abstract

We investigate the quantum entanglement dynamics of two coupled harmonic oscillators with a time-dependent interaction. Using the Lewis-Riesenfeld invariant method, we derive the exact analytical wave functions without any perturbative or adiabatic approximations and combine this with a phase-space analysis using the Wigner function to provide a complete description of the system's quantum state evolution. We obtain general expression form for the purity and the linear entropy $S_L=1-\mathcal{P}$ for arbitrary excitation numbers $(n,m)$, allows a systematic study of entanglement for a large class of quantum states. We show that the entanglement dynamics is very sensitive to the interplay between the detuning parameters $θ$ and $\vartheta_2$, the frequency parameter $β_0$ and the coupling strength $ε$: the increase of detuning takes the system from slow irregular oscillations to fast and regular periodic behavior, and the stronger coupling systematically enhances both the amplitude and the average value of the linear entropy. Most importantly, for the resonance case $ω_1=ω_2=1$ and strong couplings $ε\approx 0.99$, the system shows robust undamped synchronized periodic oscillations of the linear entropy for all quantum states considered, indicating preserved quantum coherence without saturation. Our findings demonstrate that linear entropy is a sensitive and practical entanglement witness, and we establish explicit analytical relations between the coupling parameters of the system and its entanglement properties, which are directly relevant to quantum information processing and the control of quantum correlations in continuous-variable systems.


---


## 通过单个辅助子实现玻色子状态转移的双模式宇称合成

**Original Title:** Bright-mode parity synthesis for bosonic state transfer through a single ancilla

**Authors:** Pradip Laha, Peter van Loock

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29624v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29624v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

玻色子模式提供硬件高效的量子存储器和逻辑寄存器，包括高度非高斯编码的状态，但通过受限辅助接口传输有限维玻色子状态需要识别实际控制的集体模式。我们研究了一个有限的环境，其中两个振子以相反的符号耦合到一个两级辅助。在正常模式基础上，对称模式是暗模式，而物理模式之间的转移相当于在反对称明模式上合成宇称。这种简化给出了Fock状态、Fock状态量子位和有限Fock叠加的精确有限和转移公式，并解释了为什么共振单辅助转移在单量子区域之外受到回归限制。然后，我们表明，失调Jaynes-Cummings进化提供了高保真有限截止宇称合成的原生双参数路径，并分别量化了剩余辅助激励、校准灵敏度和最小马尔科夫噪音估计。玻色子码示例说明了传输灵敏度如何受到光子数支持和残余明模相差的控制。当直接交换不可用或不受欢迎时，该结果为受限制的辅助介导的脑体转移提供了实用的基准和组织原则。


### Abstract

Bosonic modes provide hardware-efficient quantum memories and logical registers, including highly non-Gaussian encoded states, but transferring finite-dimensional bosonic states through a restricted ancilla interface requires identifying which collective mode is actually controlled. We study a restricted setting in which two oscillators couple with opposite signs to a single two-level ancilla. In the normal-mode basis, the symmetric mode is dark, while transfer between the physical modes is equivalent to synthesizing parity on the antisymmetric bright mode. This reduction gives exact finite-sum transfer formulas for Fock states, Fock-state qubits, and finite Fock superpositions, and explains why resonant single-ancilla transfer is recurrence-limited beyond the single-photon sector. We then show that detuned Jaynes--Cummings evolution provides a native two-parameter route to high-fidelity finite-cutoff parity synthesis, with residual ancilla excitation, calibration sensitivity, and a minimal Markovian noise estimate quantified separately. Bosonic-code examples illustrate how transfer sensitivity is governed by photon-number support and residual bright-mode phase errors. The result provides a practical benchmark and organizing principle for constrained ancilla-mediated bosonic transfer when direct exchange is unavailable or undesirable.


---


## 非线性介质表征中非高斯优势的压缩催化剂

**Original Title:** Squeezing as a catalyst for non-Gaussian advantage in characterization of nonlinear media

**Authors:**  Manju, Samaneh Hesabi, Siting Tang, Peter van Loock, Matteo G. A. Paris

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29633v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29633v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

我们使用相干和压缩真空态作为高斯探针，以及它们的附加光和减光对应物作为非高斯探针，解决了连续变量（CV）量子系统中非线性媒体耦合强度的精确描述。我们考虑三类主要的非线性Hamilton，即积分非线性、广义压缩和克尔型相互作用。通过分析评估量子费舍尔信息（QFI），我们比较了高斯和非高斯探针的性能，并根据探针参数、能源和非高斯性评估最佳探针。我们的结果如下：首先，对于相干态家族，固定相干幅度下的量子叠加所提供的改进主要来自探针携带的额外能量，而不提供真正的拉曼资源，因为相同的精度可以通过更大能量的高斯相干态信号来实现，这可以更容易地产生。其次，相比之下，当应用于压缩真空状态等已经非经典的状态时，量子加法和减法就成为有效的资源。在这种情况下，它们导致QFI的显着增强，特别是对于更高级的相互作用。尽管高斯压缩态在等能量约束下仍然是最佳的，但添加光和减去光的压缩态实现了相当的灵敏度，压缩要求明显较低。由于大的压缩水平在实验上仍然具有挑战性，这些非高斯探测器提供了一种实用的途径，以增强当前可用的压缩区域内的非线性耦合强度的估计。


### Abstract

We address the precise characterization of coupling strength of nonlinear media in continuous-variable (CV) quantum systems using coherent and squeezed vacuum states as Gaussian probes, together with their photon-added and photon-subtracted counterparts as non-Gaussian probes. We consider three main classes of nonlinear Hamiltonians, namely quadrature nonlinearities, generalized squeezing and Kerr-type interactions. By analytically evaluating the quantum Fisher information (QFI), we compare the performance of Gaussian and non-Gaussian probes and assess the optimal probe based on the probe parameters, energy resource and non-Gaussianity. Our results are twofold as follows: first, for coherent-state family, the improvement provided by photon addition at fixed coherent amplitude originates mainly from the extra energy carried by the probe and does not provide a genuine metrological resource, since the same precision can be achieved by a Gaussian coherent-state signal of a larger energy, which can be more easily produced. Second, in contrast, photon addition and subtraction become effective resources when applied to already nonclassical states such as squeezed vacuum states. In this case, they lead to a significant enhancement of the QFI, particularly for higher-order interactions. Although Gaussian squeezed states remain optimal at equal energy constraint, photon-added and photon-subtracted squeezed states achieve comparable sensitives with significantly lower squeezing requirements. Since large squeezing level remains experimentally challenging, these non-Gaussian probes offer a practical route towards enhanced estimation of the nonlinear coupling strength within currently accessible squeezing regimes.


---


## 硬件感知量子电路合成的李群扩散模型

**Original Title:** Lie Group Diffusion Models for Hardware-Aware Quantum Circuit Synthesis

**Authors:** Jyotirmai Singh

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29636v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29636v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

量子计算中的一项重要任务是与物理硬件约束兼容的么正电路合成。这个问题具有自然的混合结构，因为局部单量子位门是李群$SU（2）$上的连续变量，而纠缠电路结构是离散的且依赖于硬件。在这项工作中，我们使用生成模型来执行量子电路合成，其中结合了量子门的自然$SU（2）$多管几何形状和决定整体电路结构的硬件约束。我们的模型由两个部分组成：选择纠缠电路的电路骨架选择器和通过在弯曲的管形上执行扩散来在给定的电路模板上生成量子门的扩散模型$\mathrm{SU（2）} \simeq S ' 3 $本身。我们通过物理激励的三量子位Hamilton模拟目标（例如横向场伊辛模型和海森堡-XXZ模型）的统一编译来证明这种方法，并表明李群扩散优于可比基线。合成的电路还可以根据限制进行定制，我们通过为相同的目标单位进化生产具有大和小门旋转角的电路来证明这一点。我们还研究了合成门的一致性-复杂性边界，以证明电路选择器学会选择平衡保真度与复杂性的电路，而不是陷入最广泛的纠缠模板。这些结果表明李群扩散为硬件感知的量子电路合成提供了一个自然的生成框架。


### Abstract

An important task in quantum computing is unitary circuit synthesis compatible with physical hardware constraints. This problem has a natural hybrid structure as local single-qubit gates are continuous variables on the Lie group $SU(2)$ while the entangling circuit structure is discrete and hardware-dependent. In this work, we use generative models to perform quantum circuit synthesis incorporating both the natural $SU(2)$ manifold geometry of quantum gates and hardware constraints that determine the overall circuit structure. Our model comprises two components: a circuit skeleton selector that chooses an entangling circuit and a diffusion model that generates quantum gates on the given circuit template by performing diffusion on the curved manifold $\mathrm{SU(2)} \simeq S^3$ itself. We demonstrate this approach with unitary compilation of physically motivated three-qubit Hamiltonian simulation targets such as the Transverse Field Ising Model and the Heisenberg-XXZ Model and show that Lie group diffusion outperforms comparable baselines. The synthesised circuits can also be customised subject to constraints, which we demonstrate by producing circuits with large and small gate rotation angles for the same target unitary evolution. We also investigate the fidelity-complexity frontier of the synthesised gates to demonstrate that the circuit selector learns to select circuits that balance fidelity with complexity rather than collapsing onto the most expansive entangling template. These results demonstrate that Lie group diffusion provides a natural generative framework for hardware-aware quantum circuit synthesis.


---


## 利用基于中间电路测量的周期基准来描述不可学习的噪音

**Original Title:** Characterization of Unlearnable Noise with Mid-Circuit-Measurement-Based Cycle Benchmarking

**Authors:** M. H. Cheng, Stefano Mangini, V. Bartsch, A. C. Medina, Sergey N. Filippov, Matteo A. C. Rossi, M. S. Kim

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29638v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29638v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

多量子位纠缠Clifford操作的噪音特征是量子误差缓解以及量子误差纠正协议的校准、验证和优化的关键实际瓶颈，尤其是在存在状态准备和测量（SPAM）错误的情况下。尽管循环基准测试可以隔离一些泡利误差分量，但它无法解决耦合误差参数的问题，这会导致即使在简单的有噪门中也无法学习的自由度，更不用说一般的$n$-qubit Clifford门了。在这里，我们引入了基于中间电路测量的广义周期基准测试，这是一个框架，通过重复测量和经典后处理，可以学习否则无法识别的泡利概率和非马尔科夫噪音。将延迟反馈原理应用于广义周期基准测试，我们表明插入中间电路测量可以逆转由一般克利福德门引起的泡利周期。这一事实使我们能够揭示克利福德门的保利噪音可学习性条件。假设有足够的状态准备质量，我们用数字方式证明了描述以前不可学习的噪音成分的可行性。我们在超导量子处理单元上实现了该协议，并验证了其在消除耦合噪音成分歧义方面的有效性，并以传统断层扫描为基准。最后，我们观察到一致的测量引起的位翻转偏差和非马尔科夫相关性，这定义了泡利噪音模型和拟议的噪音特征化协议的适用范围。


### Abstract

Noise characterization of multi-qubit entangling Clifford operations is a key practical bottleneck for quantum error mitigation and for the calibration, validation, and optimization of quantum error-correction protocols, especially in the presence of state preparation and measurement (SPAM) errors. Although cycle benchmarking can isolate some Pauli error components, it cannot resolve the problem of coupled error parameters, which leads to unlearnable degrees of freedom even in simple noisy gates, not to mention general $n$-qubit Clifford gates. Here we introduce mid-circuit-measurement-based generalized cycle benchmarking, a framework that makes otherwise unidentifiable Pauli fidelities and non-Markovian noise learnable via repeated measurements and classical post-processing. Applying the deferred feed-forward principle to generalized cycle benchmarking, we show that an insertion of mid-circuit measurements can reverse Pauli cycles induced by a general Clifford gate. This fact enables us to reveal a Pauli-noise learnability condition for Clifford gates. Assuming sufficient state preparation quality, we numerically demonstrate the feasibility of characterizing the previously unlearnable noise components. We implement the protocol on superconducting quantum processing units and validate its effectiveness in disambiguating the coupled noise components, benchmarked against conventional tomography. Finally, we observe consistent measurement-induced bit-flip bias and non-Markovian correlations, which define a range of applicability for the Pauli noise model and the proposed noise-characterization protocol.


---


## 混合量子近邻选择：通过随机前沿分解的NISQ兼容组合优化

**Original Title:** Hybrid Quantum Neighborhood Selection: NISQ-Compatible Combinatorial Optimization via Stochastic Frontier Decomposition

**Authors:** Nicolas Mendes de Araujo, Lester de Abreu Faria

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29647v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29647v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-28


### 摘要

大规模组合优化对短期量子计算来说是一个挑战，因为密集的二次无约束二进制优化（QUBO）公式产生的相互作用图超出了NISQ处理器的限制。这项工作引入了混合量子邻居选择（HQNS），这是一个通过随机前沿分解来缓解这种情况的混合框架。HQNS没有将所有N个变量编码到单片电路中，而是选择每级F << N个有效变量的紧凑前沿，将其余变量冻结为减少的QUBO系数。多阶段爬行过程旋转这些边界，让局部量子子问题完善全局解决方案。我们在六个尺度（N至1000）上评估HQNS的最大多样性子集选择问题（MDSDP）。电路负担从每层O（N#2）两量子位项的密集QAOA要求减少到每级O（F#2），总复杂性由级数量和经典开销决定。基准测试表明，HQNS实现了相对于并行模拟退变（SA）有竞争力的解决方案质量，同时保持有界电路宽度和稳定的QPU时间。在十次执行的N=1000基准中，HQNS保留了11次重启并行SA基线平均多样性得分的99.9908%，同时减少了65.03%的壁挂时间，减少了55.97%的峰值中央处理器使用率，减少了35.21%的峰值内存。消融显示性能取决于前沿尺寸、热启动、CVaR过滤和随机旋转。这些结果表明，结构化前沿分解使得变分优化对于密集QUBO实例可执行，不适合当前硬件上的直接QAOA。


### Abstract

Large-scale combinatorial optimization is a challenge for near-term quantum computing because dense Quadratic Unconstrained Binary Optimization (QUBO) formulations yield interaction graphs that exceed the limits of NISQ processors. This work introduces Hybrid Quantum Neighborhood Selection (HQNS), a hybrid framework mitigating this via stochastic frontier decomposition. Instead of encoding all N variables into a monolithic circuit, HQNS selects a compact frontier of F << N active variables per stage, freezing the rest into reduced QUBO coefficients. A multi-stage crawling procedure rotates these frontiers, letting local quantum subproblems refine a global solution. We evaluate HQNS on the Maximum Diversity Subset Selection Problem (MDSSP) across six scales, N up to 1000. Circuit burden is reduced from the dense QAOA requirement of O(N^2) two-qubit terms per layer to O(F^2) per stage, with total complexity governed by the number of stages and classical overhead. Benchmarks show that HQNS achieves competitive solution quality relative to parallel simulated annealing (SA) while maintaining bounded circuit width and stable QPU time. In the N=1000 benchmark over ten executions, HQNS preserves 99.9908% of the mean diversity score of an 11-restart parallel SA baseline, while reducing wall-clock time by 65.03%, peak CPU usage by 55.97%, and peak memory by 35.21%. Ablation shows performance depends on frontier size, warm-starts, CVaR filtering, and stochastic rotation. These results demonstrate that structured frontier decomposition makes variational optimization executable for dense QUBO instances unsuitable for direct QAOA on present hardware.


---


## 量子优化猜想的机器验证证明

**Original Title:** A Machine-Verified Proof of a Quantum-Optimization Conjecture

**Authors:** Uri Kol, Maor Ben-Shahar, Kfir Sulimany, Dirk Englund

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29687v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29687v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-29


### 摘要

我们报告了量子优化领域十多年来悬而未决的一个问题的机器验证解决方案：Farhi、Goldstone和Gutmann（FGG）猜想，即深度-$p$不一致环上的量子近似优化算法（QAOA）精确地达到逼近比$（2 p +1）/（2 p +2）$。我们使用大型语言模型Claude Fable 5找到了证明，并由Lean 4证明助手端到端验证了其正确性。我们的方法论包括几个组成部分：建立在大量的量子信息精益库的基础上，我们形式化了QAOA组件和问题的已知部分，并将猜想简化为一个开放的数学陈述。然后将该模型交给库和我们的代理工具包，并负责通过在精益中构建证明来缩小这一差距。由此产生的过程是模型的自然语言推理和Lean的机械验证之间的反馈循环，该循环收敛为机器验证的证据。仅需要对结构脚手架进行人工验证--正式声明忠实地编码了预期的主张--而证据本身由模型提供并由Lean机械认证。尽管如此，证据还是引人注目的--该模型揭示了问题隐藏的动态对称性，并利用它，借用邻近领域的工具和机器，将一个棘手的存在问题转化为一个显式的结构。这项工作为解决量子信息科学及其他领域的开放猜想铺平了道路。


### Abstract

We report a machine-verified resolution of a problem open for over a decade in quantum optimization: the Farhi, Goldstone and Gutmann (FGG) conjecture that depth-$p$ Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm (QAOA) on the ring of disagrees attains approximation ratio $(2p+1)/(2p+2)$ exactly. We found the proof using a large language model, Claude Fable 5, and verified its correctness end-to-end by the Lean 4 proof assistant. Our methodology includes several ingredients: building on a substantial Lean library of quantum information, we formalized the QAOA components and the known parts of the problem, and reduced the conjecture to a single open mathematical statement. The model was then handed the library and our agentic toolkit, and tasked with closing that gap by constructing a proof in Lean. The resulting process is a feedback loop between the model's natural-language reasoning and Lean's mechanical verification, which converged to a machine-verified proof. Human verification is required only for the structural scaffolding - that the formal statement faithfully encodes the intended claim - while the proof itself is supplied by the model and certified mechanically by Lean. The proof is nevertheless striking - the model uncovered a hidden dynamical symmetry of the problem and exploited it, borrowing tools and machinery from an adjacent field to turn a hard existence problem into an explicit construction. This work paves the way for resolving open conjectures in quantum information science and beyond.


---


## 通过高级泰勒状态进化缓解自适应VQE中的稀疏矩阵缩放瓶颈

**Original Title:** Alleviating the Sparse Matrix Scaling Bottleneck in Adaptive VQE via High-Order Taylor State Evolution

**Authors:** Hermawan Kresno Dipojono

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29692v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29692v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-29


### 摘要

变分量子特征解算器（VQE）是用于有噪的中等规模量子（NISQ）设备的领先算法，但其自适应变体（例如，ADAPT-VQE）在模拟生长阶段遇到严重的经典模拟瓶颈。为多量子位系统表示和取指数的池运算符会构建大量稀疏矩阵，这些矩阵可以快速扩展到数百万个元素，从而抑制经典内存带宽和中央处理器/图形处理器周期容量。在这项工作中，我们提出了一个资源高效的软件层框架，该框架通过确定性五阶（O（5））泰勒系列展开来评估状态更新，完全绕过了密集矩阵取指数。这种方法将代价高昂的正进化重新构建为五个轻量级、连续稀疏矩阵-载体相乘的连锁序列，严格缩放为O（Nz），其中Nz是非零元素的数量。我们使用平衡BeH 2（14个量子位）、平衡H2O（12个量子位）以及Jordan-Wigner（JW）和Bravyi-Kitaev（BK）变换下强相关的不对称拉伸H2O分子谱来验证我们的框架。模拟结果表明，O（5）截断保持了出色的数字保真度，保持了> 0.999999的状态保真度，并将绝对底价能量匹配到亚化学准确度，同时毫不费力地导航超过2.68亿个结构元素的矩阵空间。该框架提供了一种可扩展、高性能的途径，用于在计算预算有限的硬件平台上执行深度变分模拟。


### Abstract

The Variational Quantum Eigensolver (VQE) is a leading algorithm for noisy intermediate-scale quantum (NISQ) devices, but its adaptive variants (e.g., ADAPT-VQE) suffer from severe classical simulation bottlenecks during the ansatz growth phase. Representing and exponentiating pool operators for multi-qubit systems constructs massive sparse matrices that quickly scale to millions of elements, choking classical memory bandwidth and CPU/GPU cycle capacity. In this work, we present a resource-efficient software-layer framework that completely bypasses dense matrix exponentiation by evaluating state updates through a deterministic fifth-order (O(5)) Taylor series expansion. This approach reframes the costly unitary evolution into a chained sequence of five lightweight, successive sparse matrix-vector multiplications scaling strictly as O(Nz), where Nz is the number of non-zero elements. We validate our framework using equilibrium BeH2 (14 qubits), equilibrium H2O (12 qubits), and strongly correlated asymmetrically stretched H2O molecular profiles under both Jordan-Wigner (JW) and Bravyi-Kitaev (BK) transformations. The simulation results demonstrate that the O(5) truncation maintains exceptional numerical fidelity, retaining a state fidelity > 0.999999 and matching absolute ground state energies down to subchemical accuracy, while effortlessly navigating matrix spaces exceeding 268 million structural elements. This framework provides a scalable, high-performance pathway for executing deep variational simulations on hardware platforms with constrained computational budgets.


---


## 高斯玻色子采样中的量子复杂性资源：半定程序的核心结构

**Original Title:** Quantum complexity resource in Gaussian boson sampling: Core structure of the semidefinite program

**Authors:** Kunwar Kalra, Vitaly Kocharovsky

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29739v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29739v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-29


### 摘要

我们对高斯玻色子采样中玻色子模系统的量子复杂性资源的代数和几何结构进行了严格的分析。该资源是该系统量子优势的基础：其光计数统计数据需要对资源协方差矩阵进行高斯次评估，并且该计算是#P-hard的。资源协方差矩阵是半定程序的解，该程序提取总协方差矩阵的最小踪迹物理量子部分;补充部分是半定正的，因此可以经典模拟。早期的工作仅通过量子部分的踪迹（等于其量子数）来描述这种资源。我们将优化器本身描述为量子状态和几何对象，超出了其轨迹给出的纯量。我们证明它是一个唯一的纯高斯状态，并构造一个遵循代数Riccati身份的显式Oracle映射，以重建资源。我们证明了完整的问题精确地压缩到二元程序支持产生的活动辛部门上。被动对角化状态以封闭形式（第一个显式可解类）求解，并且整个程序被证明相当于辛群（即西格尔上半空间）上的最小化。这些结果共同确定了该程序确定了资源的典型局部纯高斯分量，并为其详细分析提供了结构基础。


### Abstract

We present a rigorous analysis of the algebraic and geometric structure of the quantum complexity resource of a system of bosonic modes in Gaussian boson sampling. This resource underlies the quantum advantage of the system: its photon-counting statistics require the evaluation of a hafnian of the resource covariance matrix, and that computation is #P-hard. The resource covariance matrix is the solution of a semidefinite program that extracts the minimum-trace physical quantum part of the total covariance matrix; the complementary part is positive semidefinite and can therefore be simulated classically. Earlier work characterized this resource only through the trace of the quantum part, equal to its photon number. We characterize the optimizer itself, as a quantum state and as a geometric object, beyond the scalar given by its trace. We prove that it is a unique pure Gaussian state and construct an explicit oracle map, obeying an algebraic Riccati identity, that reconstructs the resource. We prove that the full problem compresses exactly onto the active symplectic sector that the dual program support generates. The passive-diagonalizable states are solved in closed form, the first explicit solvable class, and the whole program is shown to be equivalent to a minimization over the symplectic group, that is, over the Siegel upper half-space. Together these results establish that the program determines a canonical localized pure Gaussian component of the resource, and they provide the structural foundation for its detailed analysis.


---


## 通过逆转Trotter误差动力学进行无偏Hamilton模拟

**Original Title:** Unbiased Hamiltonian Simulation by Reversing Trotter Error Dynamics

**Authors:** Keisuke Murota, Yuta Kikuchi, Enrico Rinaldi, Frédéric Sauvage, Synge Todo

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29741v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29741v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-29


### 摘要

由于其简单性和低成本，铃木-特罗特公式仍然是当前量子计算平台上事实上的汉密尔顿模拟方法。然而，当扩展到更大的问题并寻求更高的准确性时，系统性Trotter误差很快就会变得有限。我们提出了一种机制，可以消除任何$k阶Suzuki-Trotter模拟的系统误差，但代价是恒定的采样费用。关键的见解是，特罗特误差本身就是一个需要逆转的连贯动态，而不是一个需要限制的偏差。通过以适当的形式识别该错误的结构，我们通过准概率分解来实现逆转。由此产生的算法称为概率Trotter误差逆转器（PTER），它是无偏的，与Suzuki-Trotter公式相比改进了门计数缩放，并且仍然保留了其简单性。海森堡旋转链的数值模拟已经支持了中等系统规模下预测的资源优势。Keisuke Murota、Yuta Kikuchi、Enrico Rinaldi、Frédéric Sauvage、Synge Todo


### Abstract

Owing to their simplicity and low overhead, Suzuki--Trotter formulas remain the de facto Hamiltonian simulation methods on current quantum computing platforms. Systematic Trotter errors, however, will quickly become limiting when scaling to larger problems and aiming for higher accuracy. We present a mechanism that removes the systematic error of any $k$-th order Suzuki--Trotter simulation, at the cost of a constant sampling overhead. The key insight is that the Trotter error is itself a coherent dynamics to be reversed, rather than a deviation to be bounded. By identifying the structure of this error in a suitable form, we carry out that reversal through quasi-probabilistic decompositions. The resulting algorithm, called Probabilistic Trotter Error Reversal (PTER), is unbiased, improves the gate-count scaling compared to Suzuki--Trotter formulas, and still retains their simplicity. Numerical simulations of a Heisenberg spin chain support the predicted resource advantage already at modest system sizes.Keisuke Murota, Yuta Kikuchi, Enrico Rinaldi, Frédéric Sauvage, Synge Todo


---


## 腔-QED系统中双量子产生的相关操纵

**Original Title:** Coherent manipulation of the biphoton generation in cavity-QED system

**Authors:** Jia-Ni Yang, Xin-Yi Ling, Yuan Feng, Xiao-Jun Zhang, Jin-Hui Wu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29764v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29764v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-29


### 摘要

本文从理论上研究了单原子腔QED系统中通过自发四波混频产生双光子的相干操纵。原子被泵浦场、耦合场和驱动场驱动，两个腔增强了斯托克斯和反斯托克斯光子的产生。通过求解稳态下的主方程，分析了光谱亮度，以及自相关和互相关的程度。结果表明，当泵浦场和驱动场处于双光子共振时，暗态建立在基态和里德伯态之间。有效地增强了驱动场对双量子产生和量子统计的可控性。相比之下，在大的双量子失调下，驱动场的控制能力显着降低。与电磁感应透明度直接相关的耦合场修改了双子的谱线宽度，而原子-腔耦合强度只改变亮度，而不影响谱线宽度。


### Abstract

We theoretically investigate the coherent manipulation of biphoton generation via spontaneous four-wave mixing in a cavity-QED system with a single atom. The atom is driven by pumping, coupling, and driving fields, and the generation of the Stokes and anti-Stokes photons are enhanced by two cavities. By solving the master equation in the steady state, we analyze the spectral brightness, as well as the degree of the auto-correlation and cross-correlation. Our results show that when the pumping and driving fields are in two-photon resonance, the dark state established between the ground and Rydberg states. efficiently enhances the controllability of the driving field over the biphoton generation and the quantum statistics. In contrast, under large two-photon detuning, the control capability of the driving field is significantly reduced. The coupling field, which directly relates to the electromagnetically induced transparency, modifies the linewidth of the biphoton, while the atom-cavity coupling strength only changes the brightness without affecting the linewidth.

## PPT和CCNR标准的量子电路实现

**Original Title:** Quantum Circuit Realization of the PPT and CCNR Criteria

**Authors:** Jihui Mo, Yuanhong Tao

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29769v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29769v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-29


### 摘要

量子纠缠的有效检测是量子信息处理的核心问题。本文系统地提出了一种基于正部分转置（PPT）和可计算交叉规范重新排列（CCNR）准则的量子电路实现方案，为高效且可计算的纠缠检测提供了完整的量子算法路径。通过将量子状态编码为特定形式并利用SWAP操作，部分转置和重新排列等复杂矩阵操作被转化为可执行的量子电路。此外，通过集成改进的变分量子奇异值分解子程序，该方案能够有效估计踪迹范，从而确定纠缠的存在。该方案旨在在混合量子-经典框架下运行，具有出色的可扩展性和实用性，为分析未来中等规模量子设备上复杂量子系统的纠缠结构提供了理论工具和方法论支持。


### Abstract

The efficient detection of quantum entanglement is a central problem in quantum information processing. This paper systematically proposes a quantum circuit implementation scheme based on the Positive Partial Transpose (PPT) and the Computable Cross-Norm Realignment (CCNR) criteria, providing a complete quantum algorithmic pathway for efficient and computable entanglement detection. By encoding quantum states into specific forms and utilizing SWAP operations, complex matrix operations such as partial transpose and realignment are transformed into executable quantum circuits. Furthermore, by integrating an improved variational quantum singular value decomposition subroutine, the scheme enables the efficient estimation of the trace norm, thereby determining the existence of entanglement. Designed to operate within a hybrid quantum-classical framework, this scheme exhibits excellent scalability and practicality, offering a theoretical tool and methodological support for analyzing the entanglement structure of complex quantum systems on future intermediate-scale quantum devices.

## 非惯性量子系统中的Krylov复杂性

**Original Title:** Krylov Complexity in Non-Inertial Quantum Systems

**Authors:** Ming-Qi Ma, Shi-Cheng Liu, Lei-Hua Liu, Hai-Qing Zhang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29770v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29770v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-29


### 摘要

在这项工作中，我们在非惯性量子系统中公式化了Krylov复杂性，$SU（1，1）$部门从Klein-Gordon辛形式中直接出现，这表明林德勒对数部门自然形成了均匀加速观察者的Krylov基。在这种结构下，我们通过利用$SU（1，1）$群结构Hamilton来推广Bogoliubov系数。在这个框架内，我们明确地推导出Krylov复杂度完全等于通过Bogoliubov混合生成的相关Rindler对的平均数。此外，汉密尔顿量中的失调参数和对产生参数之间的竞争将动力学分为三个不同的区域：双曲Krylov传播、临界增长和有界Krylov空间运动。值得注意的是，在失调主导的体制中，对数分布仍然以指数形式限制在低Krylov水平，这意味着波包被困在低水平，这体现为Krylov复杂性的局部化。最终，我们的工作为非惯性量子系统中Krylov复杂性的结构构建提供了新的线索。


### Abstract

In this work, we formulate the Krylov complexity in non-In an inertial quantum system, the direct emergence of the $SU(1,1)$ sector from the Klein-Gordon symplectic form dictates that the Rindler pair-number sector naturally forms the Krylov basis for uniformly accelerating observers. Under this construction, we generalize the Bogoliubov coefficients by exploiting the $SU(1,1)$ group-structured Hamiltonian. Within this framework, we explicitly derive that the Krylov complexity is exactly equal to the mean number of correlated Rindler pairs generated via Bogoliubov mixing. Furthermore, the competition between the detuning parameter and the pair-production parameter in the Hamiltonian separates the dynamics into three distinct regimes: hyperbolic Krylov spreading, critical growth, and bounded Krylov-space motion. Notably, in the detuning-dominated regime, the pair-number distribution remains exponentially confined to low Krylov levels, implying that the wave packet becomes trapped at low levels, which manifests as the localization of Krylov complexity. Ultimately, our work sheds new light on the structural construction of Krylov complexity in non-inertial quantum systems.


---


## 通过本地测量计划进行多方量子资源蒸馏

**Original Title:** Multipartite quantum resource distillation through local measurement programs

**Authors:** Yan Wang, Shao-Qi Lin, Xi-Nuo Tao, Li-Jiong Shen, Yong-Nan Sun, Ze-Yan Hao, Kai Sun, Qi-Ping Su, Chui-Ping Yang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29772v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29772v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-29


### 摘要

实际多用户量子网络中的分布式量子资源不可避免地会受到环境噪声、信道损耗和设备缺陷的影响。为了解决这些问题，量子资源蒸馏提供了一种从不完美状态中恢复更强大资源的基本方法。然而，传统的实现往往需要额外的副本，专用的物理过滤元件，或限制到二分系统，可扩展的多部网络带来的挑战。在这里，我们介绍了基于局域测量程序（LMP）的量子资源蒸馏方法，该方法将完全正映射转换为可编程的测量过程。我们通过实验证明了通过LMP在二分和三分光系统中进行资源蒸馏的性能，包括激活和增强多方操纵配置。为了展示LMP框架的灵活性和可扩展性，我们还表明虚拟资源蒸馏可以在其中自然地重新制定。我们的结果建立了一种可编程且实验经济的方法，用于在多方和更高维度系统中提取量子资源，从而提供了通往可扩展量子网络的实用途径。


### Abstract

Distributed quantum resources in practical multi-user quantum networks are inevitably degraded by environmental noise, channel loss, and device-induced imperfections. To address these issues, quantum resource distillation offers a fundamental approach to recovering stronger resources from imperfect states. However, conventional implementations often require additional copies, dedicated physical filtering elements, or restrict to bipartite systems, posing challenges for scalable multipartite networks. Here, we introduce the method of quantum resource distillation based on the local measurement program (LMP), which transfers completely positive maps into programmable measurement processes. We experimentally demonstrate the performance of resource distillation through LMP in both bipartite and tripartite photonic systems, including the activation and enhancement of multipartite steering configurations. To demonstrate the flexibility and extensibility of the LMP framework, we also show that virtual resource distillation can be naturally reformulated within it. Our results establish a programmable and experimentally economical approach for distilling quantum resources in multipartite and higher-dimensional systems, thereby providing a practical route toward scalable quantum networks.


---


## 通过局部量子费舍尔信息的非局部效应：特征化和解释

**Original Title:** Nonlocal effects via Local Quantum Fisher Information: Characterizations and Interpretations

**Authors:** R. Muthuganesan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29795v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29795v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-29


### 摘要

本文提出了一种基于量子Fisher信息的测量诱导非定域性（QFI-MIN），它量化了由局部不变幺正动力学引起的最大统计非定域性。建议的措施继承了理想的属性，包括积极性，局部酉不变性，单调性下的局部操作，和免疫力的局部附属问题。得到了纯态、任意两量子比特态和两量子比特X态的解析表达式，揭示了纯系统纠缠的直接联系。我们进一步建立QFI-MIN在量子参数估计，本地信道鉴别和相关辅助通信中的清晰操作解释。它在幅度衰减、去极化和广义幅度衰减通道下的行为表现出了对环境噪音的鲁棒性。提出的框架提供了物理上一致且具有操作意义的量子相关性量化器，将非定域性、量子计量学和量子信息处理联系起来


### Abstract

We introduce a quantum Fisher information based measurement-induced nonlocality (QFI-MIN), which quantifies the maximal statistical distinguishability induced by locally invariant unitary dynamics. The proposed measure inherits desirable properties including positivity, local unitary invariance, monotonicity under local operations, and immunity to the local ancilla problem. Analytical expressions are obtained for pure states, arbitrary two-qubit states, and two-qubit X states, revealing a direct connection with entanglement for pure systems. We further establish clear operational interpretations of QFI-MIN in quantum parameter estimation, local channel discrimination, and correlation-assisted communication. Its behavior under amplitude damping, depolarizing, and generalized amplitude damping channels demonstrates robustness against environmental noise. The proposed framework provides a physically consistent and operationally meaningful quantifier of quantum correlations, linking nonlocality, quantum metrology, and quantum information processing


---


## ZX图中的红外安全性：软QED作为开放量子系统的绝对证明

**Original Title:** Infrared Safety from ZX-Diagrams: A Categorical Proof of Soft-QED as Open Quantum System

**Authors:** Soo-Jong Rey

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29804v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29804v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-29


### 摘要

废弃的ZX演算是混合状态量子力学的一种图形语言，用于为QED中红外分歧的布洛赫-诺德西克抵消提供非微扰、绝对证明。软量子被视为开放量子系统：分解的带电粒子和硬量子形成系统，而低于探测器分辨率的量子形成环境。简化的硬通道是完全正痕迹保留（CPTP）地图，软量子定理用受控位移操作符取代了完整的S-矩阵，其费曼-弗农影响函式满足等历史正规化${\calF}[J，J]=1 $。在ZX演算中，这种规范化是一个单一的图形身份：双倍位移图在正性、循环性和丢弃规则下折叠成裸线。因此，该证明可以作为对配套论文中给出的软QED开放系统处理的绝对一致性检查;它证实物理推导在逻辑上是完整的，并且没有关于红外极限的隐藏假设。对于非对角线硬状态元素，相同的图产生了相关状态重叠，给出了软云去相关的第一性原理解释。然后将软壳粗粒化构建为CPTP Schur通道，其无限小极限产生精确的Lindblad生成器，其跳跃操作符由Eikonal发射幅度确定。最后，为非马尔科夫过程张量开发了本地CPTP认证管道，从而能够在开放量子模拟中对痕迹保留进行恒时验证。该框架连接了范畴量子语义、非平衡场论和实际开放系统编译。


### Abstract

The discard ZX-calculus, a diagrammatic language for mixed-state quantum mechanics, is used to give a nonperturbative, categorical proof of the Bloch-Nordsieck cancellation of infrared divergences in QED. Soft photons are treated as an open quantum system: the resolved charged particles and hard photons form the system, while photons below a detector resolution form the environment. The reduced hard channel is a completely positive trace-preserving (CPTP) map, and the soft-photon theorem replaces the full S-matrix by a controlled displacement operator whose Feynman-Vernon influence functional satisfies the equal-history normalization ${\cal F}[J,J]=1 $. In the ZX-calculus, this normalization is a single diagrammatic identity: the doubled displacement diagram collapses to the bare wire under the unitarity, cyclicity, and discard rules. The proof therefore serves as a categorical consistency check on the open-system treatment of soft QED given in a companion paper; it confirms that the physical derivation is logically complete and free of hidden assumptions about the infrared limit. For off-diagonal hard-state elements, the same diagram yields the coherent-state overlap, giving a first-principles account of soft-cloud decoherence. The soft-shell coarse graining is then constructed as a CPTP Schur channel whose infinitesimal limit produces the exact Lindblad generator with jump operators determined by the eikonal emission amplitudes. Finally, a local CPTP-certification pipeline is developed for non-Markovian process tensors, enabling constant-time verification of trace preservation in open quantum simulations. The framework bridges categorical quantum semantics, non-equilibrium field theory, and practical open-system compilation.


---


## 2D蜂窝Sierpiğski分数线中的Spin-1 Dirac分散和Chern绝缘相

**Original Title:** Spin-1 Dirac dispersion and Chern insulating phases in 2D honeycomb Sierpiński fractal

**Authors:** Shneha Biswas, Shouya Yoshida, Katsunori Wakabayashi, Sudipta Dutta

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.29827v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.29827v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-29


### 摘要

基于Graffene的Sierpiğski分数线在最近邻紧束缚模型中承载零能手征模式和旋转为1的Dirac分散体。然而，由局部通量和交错塞门诺夫质量项（在霍尔丹Hamilton中建模）引起的复杂次近邻跳变的存在，分别打破了时间反转和空间反转对称性，并使这些平带分散。此外，他们在这类系统中引入了丰富的拓扑相，这些系统可以用高达$\PM 3$的陈数来描述，即，超越传统的蜂窝网格。这些观察结果为探索石墨烯以外的2D周期性分形铺平了道路，其中可以通过外部应用场实现拓扑相转变。


### Abstract

Graphene-based Sierpiński fractals host a zero-energy chiral mode and spin-1 Dirac dispersions within the nearest-neighbor tight-binding model. However, the presence of complex next-nearest neighbor hopping arising from the local flux and the staggered Semenoff mass terms, modeled within the Haldane Hamiltonian, breaks the time-reversal and spatial inversion symmetries, respectively, and makes these flat bands dispersive. Moreover, they introduce rich topological phases in this class of systems that can be characterized by Chern numbers up to $\pm 3$, i.e., beyond the conventional honeycomb lattice. These observations pave the way for the exploration of 2D periodic fractals beyond graphene, where topological phase transitions can be realized through externally applied fields.
